SatakOpar himself has said “a*dikkIzh amarndhu pugundhu* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 6.10.11) and hence he represents the pAdhukA status of SrI ranganAthan. In addition to being the pAdhukA, [SatakOpar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) actually relishes the fact that he serves as HIS pAdhukA, as seen in his other phrases “*mugil vaNNan adiyai adaindhu* (thiruvAimozhi 7.2.11) and “uRRen ugandhu paNi seydhu ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.8.10)”. Now, the relationship between such [SatakOpar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) and [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is being described. The divine lotus feet of [SatakOpar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) is fragrant with fresh flowers that oozes honey. As [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) described “*mEvinEn avan ponnadi meymaiyE* ([kanninun chiRuth thAmbu 2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu-2-navinal/))”, [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) opined that it behooves him to be at the lotus feet of satakOpar. Hence, [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is being celebrated as the sandals of SatakOpar. Finally, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) establishes the link between him and [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) states that it is [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is responsible for his soul’s true sustenance in the first place. He advises his heart that it needs to go and surrender and live at the lotus feet of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), who is also known as [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) advises his heart similar to how [thiruvarangaththu amudhanAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/amudhanar/) adviced his heart as “*irAmusan charaNAravindham nAm manni vAzha nenjE* [(irAmAnusan nURRandhAdhi 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-1/))”. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) tells his “ Oh my heart who listens and acts according to what adiyEn says! go and be in close connection to the lotus feet of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)and expect nothing in return. It is just your svarUpam to be at the lotus feet of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)”. Since [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is characterized as epitome of love towards [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s lotus feet, he is often called as “yathIndra pravaNar”. The phrase “selvach chatakOpar” earlier refers to the wealth of [SatakOpar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/). As per the phrase “*dhanammadhIyam thava pAdha pankajam* (sthOthra rathnam)”, which says that the greatest wealth one can beget is the lotus feet of the Lord. Since [SatakOpar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) had it, he is described as “selvach chatakOpar”.


## Arththi Prabandham – ११
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/06/arththi-prabandham-10/)

[![vaduganambi-avatharasthalam](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/vaduganambi-avatharasthalam.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/vaduganambi-avatharasthalam.jpg)[vaduga nambi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/01/vaduga-nambi/)

**Introduction**

In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) assumes that [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) asks him a question. The question is “hey!!! [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)! As per the phrases ‘*nizhalum adithArumAnOm* (periya thiruvandhAdhi 31)’, ‘*mEvinEn avan ponnadi* ([kaNNinuN chiRuth thAmbu 2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu-2-navinal/))” and ‘*rAmAnuja padhachchAyA (*embAr’s thaniyan)*‘*, you yearned for the state of those devotees who are the embodiment of pArathanthriyam”. (pArathanthriyam is a quality by which the servant (owned) is completely dependent on the master(owner). The master uses the servant at his will and the servant because of his true nature does not voice any concern at any time.) [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) continues, “this kind of connection with me is only possible for the likes of [vaduga nambi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/01/vaduga-nambi/)”. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) answers to this by saying that “hey [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)!!! Please give me the state of vaduga nambi who knew no god apart from you. Please inculcate that state in me. After doing that, please use me in whatever way you want to for how much ever time you desire”.

**pAsuram:**  
unnaiyozhiya oru dheivam maRRaRiyA  
mannupugazhsEr vaduga nambi than nilayai  
enRanakku nI thandhu ethirAsA ennALum  
unRanakkE AtkoL ugandhu

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-11)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings:**  
ethirAsA – Oh! [emperumAnAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/emperumanar/)E!!!  
nI thandhu – You should give  
enRanakku – me (who yearns the state of [vaduga nambi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/01/vaduga-nambi/))  
nilayai – the charama parva nishtai (the ultimate state in which one considers his guru as his everything) state of the one who  
mannu – forever  
sEr – attained  
pugazh – glory (and who is known as)  
vaduganambi than – vaduga nambi who  
unnai ozhiya – excepting you  
oru dheivam maRRaRiyA – knew none other than you and who considered even the Lord as his hurdle because the Lord may be an interruption for him to do uninhibited service to you  
AtkoL ugandhu – (Oh! emperumAnArE) Please use me happily for your service.  
ennALum –at all times and  
unRanakkE – for you only.  
**Simple Translation:**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), in this pAsuram, requests [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) to bless him the state of [vaduga nambi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/01/vaduga-nambi/). [vaduga nambi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/01/vaduga-nambi/) was a Sishya of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who knew no god except his guru [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) asks [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) to grant him that state and asks him to use him at his will happily. He goes ahead and says that he will be happy to serve [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) at all times.

**Explanation**:

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says “Oh! The leader of sanyAsis! Please bless me with the state of [vaduga nambi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/01/vaduga-nambi/)”. [vaduga nambi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/01/vaduga-nambi/) was a Sishya of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). He knew no other god except his guru [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). vaduga nambi considered even the periya perumAL at SrIrangam as an eternal hindrance to his kainkaryam to [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). He was unlike some people who went to both, one being perumAL and the other being the AchAryan. [vaduga nambi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/01/vaduga-nambi/) regarded his AchAryan [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) as his everything and did not pay any heed in the direction of perumAL. For this extreme devotion to [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), he is celebrated at the highest pedestal. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) continues “Oh! emperumAnArE!!! As AzhvAr said “enakkE Atchey ekkAlathum [(thiruvAimozhi 2.9.4)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/06/thiruvaimozhi-2-9-4-enakke-atchey/)“, please use me for your service only at all times. adiyEn is at your disposal and please use me for your happiness!!! Wherever you go, please take me and use me for your service and subsequent happiness!!!

The phrase “*mannu pugazh sEr vaduga nambi nilai”* can also be interpreted as “mannu nilai sEr vaduganambi”. The latter split / connotation would put the adjective “mannu nilai sEr” as the qualifier for the noun [vaduga nambi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/01/vaduga-nambi/). This would mean [vaduga nambi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/01/vaduga-nambi/) who stood in the charama parva nishtai state, that attained timeless glory.


## Arththi prabandham – १२
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-11/)

[![emperumAnAr-thiruvAimozhippiLLai-mAmunigaL](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/emperumAnAr-thiruvAimozhippiLLai-mAmunigaL.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/emperumAnAr-thiruvAimozhippiLLai-mAmunigaL.jpg)[emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) – [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) – [mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)

**Introduction**

In the previous pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) requested [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) to bless him with the state of [vaduga nambi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vaduga-nambi/). sri rAmAnuja asked him, “Oh!!! [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)!You are asking me to bless you with [vaduga nambi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/01/vaduga-nambi/)‘s state. In order for me to do that, what is the relationship that you and I have? Is there a relationship in the first place between you and me?” [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) replies to this imaginary question that he posed himself and says “Oh! [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)!!! Yes. There is a relationship between you and me. The relationship is established via adiyen’s AchAryan [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/).

**pAsuram 12**  
thesam thigazhum thiruvAimozhip piLLai  
mAsil thirumalaiyAzhvAr ennai  
nEsaththAl eppadiyE eNNi ninbAl sErththAr  
ethirAsA appadiyE nI seydharuL

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-12)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings:**

thesam – All the worlds  
thigazhum – bright and sparkling with glories  
thiruvAimozhip piLLai – thiruvAimozhip piLLAi, whose very existence and sustenance is by means of thiruvAimozhi, as revealed by his name  
mAsil – the one who is devoid of blemishes that stems from regarding oneself as AchAryan  
thirumalaiyAzhvAr – who is also known as SriSailanAtha  
ennai – me, who is recipient of his infinite compassion  
nEsaththAl – out of his mercy  
eppadiyE eNNi – he thought of how will I be liberated  
ninbAl – at your divine lotus feet that is the sole refuge of all  
sErththAr – how he got me at your lotus feet  
ethirAsA – emperumAnArE  
appadiyE nI seydharuL – You also should bless me and get me liberated  
****

**Simple Translation**

In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) requests [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) to liberate him by his divine blessings. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) raises an imaginary question in mind in which [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) asks him the reason / relationship that he shares with him in order for him to bless. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) answers that the relationship between him and [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) has been established by [thiruvAimozhippiLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/), the AchAryan of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/). He says that it was [thiruvAimozhippiLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) who showed mercy upon him and thought of an idea to liberate him. Subsequently, he showed [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) the lotus feet of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) and take them as the sole refuge in order to get liberated.

**Explanation**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) in the first two lines of this pAsuram, explains the glories of his beloved AchAryan [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/). He says to emperumAnAr, “Oh! [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! adiyEn’s AchAryan [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) surrendered at the lotus feet of [nammAzhvAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/18/nammazhwar/). Subsequently, he surrendered at your lotus feet. He did not take refuge at any other person who is not regarded as “SEshi” or master, that includes SrIvaishNava pUrvAchAryas only. He was a person who was replete with knowledge, devotion towards spiritual matters and hatred in mundane materialistic pleasures. His fame and glory was not confined to just one place but it spread across all directions in the world. As could be evinced from his name, his very sustenance and existence was through [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/). If [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) was removed, he would not live any more. He did not have any blemish including the likes of proclaiming himself as an AchAryan which is considered as a cruel deed. He, who is also known as “SailanAtha”, who showed extreme mercy and compassion towards me and thought of ways to liberate me. Subsequently, he was very happy and showed me your lotus feet in order to get liberated. adiyEn requests you to kindly show mercy upon me and liberate me from the bondage of this materialistic place.


## Arththi Prabandham – १३
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-12/)

[![Azhwars](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Azhwars.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Azhwars.jpg)

**Introduction**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)thus far, requested [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) to bless him with several things. [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s ease of accessibility is such that he blessed all those wishes to turn true. Already being vowed by SrI rAmAnuja’s ease of accessibility, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) in this pAsuram falls for the beauty of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) and sings mangaLAsAsanam (glories) to it. He does not just stop with singing mangaLams to only [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) but goes ahead and sings mangaLams to all those who have the connection with [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).

**pAsuram 13**

*ethirAsan vAzhi ethirAsan vAzhi*  
*ethirAsan vAzhi enREnREthich chadhirAga*  
*vAzhvArgaL thALiNaikkIzh vAzhvArgaL peRRiduvar*  
*AzhvArgaL thangaL aruL*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-13)

**Word-by-Word Meanings**

vAzhvArgaL – Those who lives  
thALiNaikkIzh – at the lotus feet of  
vAzhvArgaL – those who live  
chadhirAga – in an intelligent fashion  
Ethich – by singing praises (glories / mangalams) such as  
ethirAsan vAzhi – “mangaLams (glories) to ethirAsan”  
ethirAsan vAzhi – “mangaLams (glories) to ethirAsan”  
ethirAsan vAzhi – “mangaLams (glories) to ethirAsan”  
enREnRu – for a long time  
peRRiduvar – will beget the  
aruL – blessings of  
AzhvArgaL thangaL – all [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)

**Simple Explanation**

In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) describes that some people will get the blessings of all [AzhwArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/). These people are none other than those who fall at other great people who hail and singing for a long time, the glories of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) such as “long live [ethirAsa](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), long live [ethirAsa](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), long live [ethirAsa](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)”

**Explanation**

[periyAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyazhwar/) sang thirupallANdu in which he sang mangaLams to [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) in multiple dimensions. While [periyAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyazhwar/) sang mangaLams to bhagavAn, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is singing mangaLams to bhAgavathas. maNavALa mAmunigaL recognizes that there are some people who stand in “charama parva nishtai”, as revealed by “*adiyEn sadhirthEn inRE* (kaNNinun chiRuth thAmbu 5). “charama parva nishtai” is the condition in which people regard their AchAryan (guru) as their everything. [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s devotees who are in this state, always sing, “long live [ethirAsa](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), long live [ethirAsa](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), long live [ethirAsa](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)”. They sing this forever. Let us call this group “Group A”. There is another group of people (Group B) who live under the lotus feet of those people who sing “long live [ethirAsa](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), long live [ethirAsa](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), long live [ethirAsa](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)”, just like how a child is under the protective shadow of its mother.
Group B people recognize the purport of the phrase “*nin thALiNAik kIzh vAzhchchi* ([thiruvAimozhi 3](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/thiruvaimozhi-3rd-centum/).2.4)” and live in the shadow of the lotus feet of Group A people. The blessings that are being showered upon the Group B people is being discussed in the latter half of the pAsuram. [AzhvArgaL](https://pillai.koyil.org/index.php/2014/10/introduction-to-azhwars/) are counted as ten in number. [madhurakavi AzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/madhurakavi-azhwar/) and [AndAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/andal/) are counted within [nammAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) and [periyAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyazhwar/) respectively. These [AzhvArs](https://pillai.koyil.org/index.php/2014/10/introduction-to-azhwars/)[](https://pillai.koyil.org/index.php/2014/10/introduction-to-azhwars/)who are being celebrated as “*mayaRvaRa madhinalam aruLa*”*ppeRRavargaL* (thiruvAimozhi 1.1.1) . In other words, they are the recipients of the causeless mercy of [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), as a result of which their ignorance got vanished completely and knowledge about and bhakthi (devotion) towards [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) started to grow profoundly. These AzhvArs did not stop their devotion to just [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). Rather they extended their devotion to the devotees of[SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) as seen in the phrase “*ellaiyil adimaith thiRaththinil enRumEvumanaththanarAi*” (perumAL thirumozhi 2.10). People in Group B get all the blessings showered upon them from all the 10 AzhwArs. It is because of their blessings that these people in group B have steadfast belief in charama parva nishtai and will continue to be there forever. It behooves us to take cognizance of the fact that in the first pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) described these people as those who will be revered by the nithyasUris (*ayaRvarum amarargaL* (thiruvAimozhi 1.1.1)). In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) celebrates that these people in group B will be celebrated by [AzhvArs](https://pillai.koyil.org/index.php/2014/10/introduction-to-azhwars/) who are described as “*[mayaRvara madhinalam aruLa](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-1-1-1-uyarvara-uyarnalam/)“peRRavargaL* (thiruvAimozhi 1.1.1) .


## Arththi Prabandham – १४
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-13/)

[![periyaperumAL-udayavar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/periyaperumAL-udayavar.png)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/periyaperumAL-udayavar.png)

**Introduction**

This pAsuram is connected to [pAsuram 12](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/06/arththi-prabandham-12/). The previous pAsuram ([pAsuram 13](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/06/arththi-prabandham-13/)) was a deviation (prAsangikam). In [pAsuram 12](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/06/arththi-prabandham-12/), [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) asked [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), “Oh! [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)! You are telling me that you surrendered unto my feet because your AchAryan had told you to do so. You say that your act of surrender to me upon your AchAryan’s direction is the way to liberate you. Will that surrender suffice in your case? Don’t you need to have any other qualification apart from your surrender?” This is what [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) assumed [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) had in mind. To this question, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) gives an answer in this pAsuram. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)says that “Oh! [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! If a person has all the desired qualifications, then why would he fall at your feet? You are a person who blesses all those who does not have any qualifications whatsoever. Hence, refugees including me should be protected only by you. If not for you, there is no other place for us”.

**pAsuram**

*adhigAramundEl arangar irangArO*  
*adhigAram illAdhArkkanRO – ethirAsa*  
*nI iranga vEnduvadhu nIyum adhigArigaLukkE*  
*irangil en seyvOm yAm*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-14)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings**

adhigAramundEl – if one is completely qualified across the dimensions of knowledge and its subsequent practice  
arangar – [periya perumAL (SrI ranganAthan)](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)  
irangArO – will he not come down and help him?  
ethirAsa – But hey ethirAsa, you  
adhigAram illAdhArkkanRO – will step down to help out those people who does not have an iota of any of the aforementioned qualification. Is it not true?  
nI iranga vEnduvadhu – We request you to come down and help such people (including me)  
nIyum adhigArigaLukkE irangil – Even you, who is the sole refuge for all the refugees, start to help out only those people who have qualifications  
en seyvOm yAm – what do we do then?

**Simple Translation:**

In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) tells [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) that he does not have any other place to go except his ([SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s) lotus feet. [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is the only person who can save any person who does not have any refuge. [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) does not look out for any qualification in a person in order to surrender unto him. It is periya perumAL who looks out for qualification such as gyAnam (knowledge) and its associated practice (anushtAnam). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) concludes by saying that if even [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) starts to look out for qualifications, then there is absolutely no place for him and others to go.

**Explanation:**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)tells [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) “Oh [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! Look at [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/)! He blesses people like [nammAzhvAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/18/nammazhwar/)as per her request “*puNNAnthuzhAme porunIrth thiruvarangA aruLAy* (thiruviruththam 28). [nammAzhvAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/18/nammazhwar/)after being liberated by the blessings of [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/)says “*aruL sUdi uyndhavan* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 7.2.11). [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/)blesses only those people who have qualifications. But look at people like us. We do not have any such qualification. Oh the leader of all yathis (sanyAsIs)!!! You have to help people like us who have no such thing called qualification. You are the sole refuge for all those innumerable souls that have no place to go. But even if you start to look out for qualifications and help only those who have them, what qualification can people like us show in order to be recipient of your mercy? We would never be liberated forever.


## Arththi Prabandham – १५
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-14/)

[![EmperumAnar_thirukoshtiyur](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/EmperumAnar_thirukoshtiyur.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/EmperumAnar_thirukoshtiyur.jpg)[emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) – thirukkOshtiyUr

**Introduction**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) opines that he had pointed fingers at [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) for his pitiable condition and also pleaded him to get him out of his dire straits. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) paused and thought to himself that [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is one who is full of auspicious qualities as per the phrase “*irAmAnusan mikka puNNiyanE* (r[AmAnusa nURRandhAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) 91). If we catch his lotus feet with all love and devotion, without blaming him for my pitiable condition, will he not do the job automatically for us? [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) then goes ahead to explore within himself whether he has any love and devotion towards [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). After some deep research, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) comes to the conclusion that he has nothing in that regard towards [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).

**pAsuram**

*emperumAnAr thiruvadigaLE SaraNam*  
*enbadhuvE nAvuraikkum iththAl en?*  
*anbavar pAl ippOdhaLavum yAn onRum kANginRilEn*  
*eppOdhu undAvadhu ini?*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-15)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings**

nAvuraikkum – my tongue, without any love / feelings  
enbadhuvE – utter the phrase that is famously known as  
[emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) thiruvadigaLE SaraNam – “I surrender to the lotus feet of[SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), who is my owner”  
iththAl en? – what is the use of saying this (without any love and devotion, just for the sake of saying it)?  
yAn onRum kANginRilEn – I am not able to figure out any  
anbu – devotion  
avar pAl – towards him  
ippOdhaLavum – till this very moment  
eppOdhu undAvadhu ini? – if not for now, when will it blossom?

**Simple Translation**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that he has been uttering the sacred phrase “emperumAnAr thiruvadigaLE SaraNam” incessantly without any result. He says that he does not really realize the meaning of it and said it. He said it just for the sake of it and opines that there is absolutely no use saying in this fashion. Subsequently, he dives deep in his heart to explore if there is any pure devotion towards SrI rAmAnuja that may be hiding somewhere. To his utter dismay, he is not able to find any trace of it.

**Explanation  **

The phrase “emperumAnAr thiruvadigaLE SaraNam” is a soul uplifting phrase for piLLai kollikAval dhAsar. The same phrase is the sustaining force for eternal enjoyment for [sOmAsiyANdAn](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/09/somasiyandan/). However, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) feels that he too tried to utter this very same phrase that meant more than their lives for these aforementioned people. But [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that he uttered the phrase just for uttering it and did not do a deep dive into its purport. He repeatedly chanted this phrase without an iota of love and devotion towards [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)explores within his heart to find any traces of love towards [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) as revealed by the phrase “*sArndhadhen sindhaiyun thALiNaikkIzh anbuthAn migavum kUrndhadhu* ([irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) 71). He is very disappointed that he could not find an iota of pure devotion and love towards [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) even until this final days of his life. He asks himself, “if not for now, when will that love blossom, if at all there is a possibility of blossoming”. He concludes that there is absolutely no use in uttering the phrase without any love and devotion. At this juncture, we should take cognizance of the fact that[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) used the phrase “[irAmAnusAya](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) nama” in [pAsuram 2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/06/arththi-prabandham-2/). In this pAsuram, he uses the phrase “[emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) thiruvadigaLE SaraNam”. Similar to [dhvaya mahAmanthram](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2015/12/rahasya-thrayam.html), there is a [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) equivalent to it. While the phrase “[emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) thiruvadigaLE SaraNam” constitutes the first half, the phrase “[irAmAnusAya](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) nama” is the latter half.


## Arththi Prabandham – १६
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-15/)

[![emperumAnAr_thiruvadi_to_a_dumb](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/emperumAnAr_thiruvadi_to_a_dumb.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/emperumAnAr_thiruvadi_to_a_dumb.jpg)[SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) blessing a mute devotee by showing him his lotus feet

**Introduction**

In the [previous pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/06/arththi-prabandham-15/), [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)
concluded that he does not have any iota of love / devotion in his heart towards [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). In this pAsuram, he assumes that [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)asks him a question. The imaginary question that [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) asks [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)is “Oh [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)!!! You said that you do not have any love or devotion towards me. That is fine. Do you at least have the hatred towards other worldly stuff? Have you stayed out from those mundane activities that hinder your spiritual journey?” [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)replies, “No. adiyEn has not refrained from worldly stuff. Nor does adiyEn have any iota of pure love and devotion towards you. Oh [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! Your lotus feet takes one’s blemishes and treats them as luxuries. adiyEn is not sure when will adiyEn reach the greatlotus feet of yours. Only you know that and only you can let me know the day when adiyen will reach you”.

**pAsuram 16**

*AgAdhadhu IdhenRu aRindhum piRarkku uraiththum*  
*AgAdhadhE seyvan AdhalAl mOkAnthan enRU*  
*ninaiththu ennai igazhEl ethirAsA*  
*enRu unnadi sErvan yAn*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-16)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings**

aRindhum – I ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) clearly knew  
IdhenRu – that the list of things that  
AgAdhadhu – the AchAryas (gurus) described as “those to be discarded”  
piRarkku uraiththum – not stopping with that, I advised others about it  
AgAdhadhE seyvan – (On the contrary, though I proscribed others to indulge things that are not advocated by our gurus) I continued to do those religiously.  
AdhalAl – Hence  
igazhEl – Please do not condemn / discard  
ennai – me  
enRU – by  
ninaiththu – thinking and dismissing me as a  
mOkAnthan – one who is succumbed to lust  
[ethirAsA](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) – Oh [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)!!!  
enRu – When will  
yAn – I  
sErvan – reach  
un – your  
adi – lotus feet

**Simple Translation**

In the earlier pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)felt bad that he did not have any love towards [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). In this pAsuram, he feels bad because he does not have hate towards other worldly stuff. He is neither here nor there, that confounds him and makes him plead [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) to take his innumerable shortcomings (blemishes) and regard them as blessings. He concludes by saying that only [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s lotus feet can protect such a person like him and that only [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) can tell a date when he would reach him.

**Explanation:**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)says “Oh [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! I clearly know all that our ancestors have prescribed us to do. I knew them so well that I even advised others to not do things that are not told in our scriptures. I told others that they should completely renounce all those activities that are condemnable by our [AchAryas](http://acharyas.koyil.org). However, when it came to my case, what I did was strange. I continued to to all those activities daily. All those activities that our [AchAryas](http://acharyas.koyil.org) have told us to discard, all those very same activities that I asked others to not do it, I was indulged in them religiously. Hence, what I preach and what I practice are not same. Oh [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! Please do not dismiss me as a person who has fallen on this mystic tangle of lust. I do not know when will I reach you, as per [nammAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/)’s words “*en nAL yAn unnai ini vandhu kUduvan*” [(thiruvAimozhi 3.2.1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/thiruvaimozhi-3-2-munnir/)). Will I lose the opportunity to reach you forever? I, who is being succumbed to the alluring yet evil lust, is full of ignorance. I do not know when will reach you. Only you, the all-knowing, have the power to know that day. Can you let me know of the day?”


## Arththi prabandham – १७
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-16/)

[![ramanuja showing paramapadham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/ramanuja-showing-paramapadham.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/ramanuja-showing-paramapadham.jpg)

**Introduction**

In the [previous pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-16/), [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) requested sri rAmAnuja to give him a date when he would reach the latter. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) thinks that this might have triggered a thought in [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s mind and he might have had a thought in his mind. The thought is that “hey! [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/). Whenever your mortal body falls on this earth, you will reach me, as per the phrase “maraNamAnAl ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 9.10.5). You will eventually be liberated and reach the eternal abode of [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), namely paramapadham”. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) puts a question back to [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) as to what is the cause of this delay. Why should he wait till his mortal body falls at the time of death. Why can’t this be expedited right away? This is the crux of this pAsuram.

**pAsuram 17**  
*pollAngu anaiththum podhindhu koNdu nanmaiyil onRu*  
*illA enakkum ethirAsA – nallArgaL*  
*naNNum thirunAttai nAn tharuvEn enRa nI*  
*thaNNenRu irukkiradhu endhAn?*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-17)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings**  
anaiththum – (I am a person with) all possible  
pollAngu – bad deeds in the words  
podhindhu koNdu – that are etched in me strongly.  
onRu illA – (I do not have) an iota of  
nanmaiyil – good deed in me.  
ethirAsA – Oh! emperumAnArE!  
enakkum – Even for such a person like me  
nAn tharuvEn enRa nI – You had told me that you will bless me  
thirunAttai – paramapadham which is  
naNNum – a place that is worthy to be reached by  
nallArgaL – people with good character.  
thaNNenRu irukkiradhu endhAn? – What is the cause of the delay in blessing me? (the inner meaning is that maNavALa mAmunigaL who does not have any place to go and who has nothing with him, yearns to go to paramapadham as quickly as possible with sri rAmAnuja’s blessings)

**Simple Translation**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says “I am a person full of bad deeds with not even an iota of good character in me. But [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) had assured me of paramapadham to even such a lowly person like me. Oh [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)!!! You had told me that you will bless me with paramapadham. Having said so, what is the cause of your delay?”

**Explanation**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) describes himself in the first half of this pAsuram. He says that he is a very low person with nothing good about him as revealed by the phrases “*nIsanEn niRai onRumilEn* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.3.4)” and “*akruthasUkrutha*:” He is a person who is full of qualities that are directly contradictory to the uplifting and liberation of a soul. In addition to that, he is a person who had literally no good character or anything that refines his soul for the better. He is a person who is always engaged in all those activities that are condemned by the ancestors and does them repeatedly. “*prApyam archipadhAsathbis thath vishNOr paramampadham*” is a phrase that describes paramapadham as a place that is desired by the elite people who are full of good deeds and character in them. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says “Oh! emperumAnArE! You assured me that you shall grant paramapadham even to such a low person like me. You said those words realizing the relationship between us. However, I am unable to understand why is the delay in granting it? Are you thinking in your mind that I might have gone to someone else thinking they might protect me? Are you thinking that, on my own effort, I can follow other routes laid by [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) to reach him in his eternal abode of paramapadham? Oh [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! neither do I know anyone except you nor do I know any means apart from you. I do not have anything in me and I have no other place to go apart from your lotus feet. Hence, I request you to kindly grant me mOksham as soon as possible”.


## Arththi Prabandham – १८
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-17/)

[![bhagavad_ramanuja_2011_may](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/bhagavad_ramanuja_2011_may.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/bhagavad_ramanuja_2011_may.jpg)

**Introduction**

[SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) had assured [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) of fulfilling his wish of reaching paramapadham. However, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is not ready to wait it out till when it is the appropriate time as shown in the phrase “avan aruL perum aLavAvinillAdhu (thiruvAimozhi 9.9.6)”. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is experiencing the pain that [nammAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) suffered in his “UrellAm thunji” ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) (5.3). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)adds that he is doomed in the eternal darkness caused ignorance that is caused by this materialistic world. In order for this darkness to be obliterated , [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) asks the sun called [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) as to when will it eventually dawn upon him?

**pAsuram 18**

enRu vidivadhu enakku endhAi ethirAsA!  
onRum aRiginRilEn uraiyAi  
kunRAmal ippadiyE indha uyirkku enRum irulE viLaikkum  
ippavamAm nInda iravu  
****

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-18)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings**

endhAi – Oh! My beloved father!!!  
[ethirAsA](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! –
[yathirAja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) (the leader of sanyAsis)  
indha uyirkku – The soul is (immersed) in  
ippavamAm – this materialistic world  
irulE viLaikkum – that is the source of darkness and ignorance  
ippadiyE – It (soul) continues to be in this state  
enRum – forever  
kunRAmal – without showing any signs of light  
nInda iravu – (This is similar to a) very long night that ceases to dawn  
uraiyAi – (Oh!!! emperumAnArE!!! Please tell me  
enRu – when  
vidivadhu enakku – will it dawn for me?  
onRum aRiginRilEn – I have no clue about anything in this regard.

**Simple Translation**

In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) tells [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) that he is completely clueless about when would he see the light at the end of the tunnel. The soul is being engulfed by darkness forever. There seems to be no imminent light that would eradicate the ignorance of the soul that is caused by inherent dark nature of this materialistic world. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) pleads for help to his father [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) by declaring his despondency about when would it eventually dawn for him.

**Explanation**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says, “Oh my beloved father [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)!!! The leader of sanyAsis! My soul does not show any signs of improvement. It seems to have been engulfed in eternal darkness. This darkness is caused by the inherent ignorance that is associated with this world that has not an iota of brightness in it. It is because of this association with this dark world that my soul is suffering from time immemorial. This long night of samsAram (worldly pain) is described as “*avivEkha ganAnantha dhingmukhE* ([sthOthra rathnam](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/01/alavandhar/) 49). I am lost in this dark night called “samsAram” that never seems to be over and I do not see light anytime soon. I am a person who does not have any clue on what is the right direction and have been wandering randomly as per the phrase “*padha skalitham* ([sthOthra rathnam](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/01/alavandhar/) 49)”. When will the good fortune of receiving your glance, occur to me? I am one, who is verily characterized by ignorance having no idea when and how it will dawn upon me? Hey [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! You are all knowing as they say in “*nikhila kumathi mAyA sarvarI bAlasUrya:* ([yathirAja sapthathi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2015/06/05/vedhanthacharyar/) 28)”. You are sun and thus only you can get rid of this darkness that engulfs me as described in the phrase “*suprabhAthathya rajanI (*SrIvishNu purANam)”.


## Arththi Prabandham – १९
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/08/arththi-prabandham-18/)

[![emperumanar-vanamamalai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/emperumanar-vanamamalai.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/emperumanar-vanamamalai.jpg)

**Introduction**

In the [previous pAsruam](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-18/) [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) requested [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) to show light to him who is suffering in the eternal darkness and ignorance of this materialistic world. In this pAsuram, he goes ahead and says that he is being controlled by his body and so he goes in the direction that his body pulls. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that this action of his would only cast a bad image on his father [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).

**pAsuram**

*allum pagalum yAn Akkai vazhi uzhanRu*  
*sellumadhu un thEsukku thIngu anRO?*  
*nallArgaL than thanayar nIsarkku Atcheyya sagipparO*  
*endhai ethirAsA isai*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-19)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings**

endhai [ethirAsA](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) – Oh my father! [yathrirAra](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! The leader of sanyAsis  
isai – only you should take action on this.  
yAn – I,  
allum pagalum – both in the night as well as day  
Akkai vazhi uzhanRu – go in the direction that my body pulls, thereby literally being a servant to my master (my body)  
sellumadhu – The way that I go in the aforementioned path that I follow  
thIngu anRO? – does it not cast a bad image on you  
un thEsukku – and you glories?  
nallArgaL – Great souls, who lead from the front in the matters concerning brahmam,  
than thanayar – (when it comes to) their son  
nIsarkku Atcheyya sagipparO – will they tolerate (their sons) performing lowly acts to low people?

**Simple Translation**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) tells [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) about the way in which he leads his life. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that he is being controlled by his body and he just blindly goes behind whatever direction it pulls him day in and day out. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) tells [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), “Hey my father! What I am doing is extremely low act. If you do not stop this, will it not cast a bad image on you, as you are my father and me, your son is going in the ways that is not prescribed? If great mahAthmAs and great souls who are the pioneers in research matters containing brahmam (the supreme being [Sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)), if they see their sons go astray, will they tolerate it? Will they not quickly turn their attention towards them and revive them?

**Explanation**

In the first half of this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) described how he spends his life. Ideally, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) should have been spending his life by chanting the names of Sri rAmAnuja, as expounded by the phrase “u[n nAmamellAm enRannAvinuLLE allum pagalum amarum padi nalga](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-thaniyans/) (irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi thaniyan). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that he had the golden time where he could have ideally chanted the glorious names of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) day in and day out. On the contrary, during those times, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that his spent his life according to the phrase “[annAL nI thandha Akkai vazhi uzhalvEn](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/thiruvaimozhi-3-2-1-munnir-gyalam/) (thiruvAimozhi 3.2.1). The meaning of the phrase is that a person spends his life as dictated by the body that was originally bestowed upon him by [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), to lead a pious life. This body was given to perform acts prescribed in the scriptures towards [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). It is not to indulge in materialistic ways. If it does, then the bad image will be cast only upon the one who gave the body in the first place, that is [sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). This was the purport of [periyAzhvAr’s](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyazhwar/) pAsuram in his “*unakkup pani seydhirukkum thavam udayEn inippOi oruvan thanakkup paNindhu kadaithalai niRka nin sAyai azhivu kaNdAi”* ([periyAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyazhwar/) thirumozhi 5.3.3). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) asks the same question as [periyAzhvar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyazhwar/), but the only difference is that while [periyAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyazhwar/) asked [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) asks [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) that would it not cast a bad image upon him, his father? [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) justifies his statement by giving an analogy. There are very knowledgeable people who indulge spend their life in thinking of the ulterior path and motive in [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). If, for some reason, their sons go astray and lead a treacherous life, will their fathers approve it? Will they accept their sons’ low condescending acts performed towards inferior people? They would never approve of it. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) tells his father[SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), “Hey my father!! The leader of sanyAsIs. You yourself had mentioned of this fact and case in hand. Hence, I request you to take me into your fold, take services from me and protect this soul. Only you can do it”.


## Arththi Prabandham – २०
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-19/)

[![going-to-paramapadham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/going-to-paramapadham.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/going-to-paramapadham.jpg)

**Introduction:**

In the [previous pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-19/), [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) asked [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) whether knowledgeable people would tolerate their sons going astray. [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is described as, the one who is pursued by good persons as per the phrase “*nallAr paravum irAmAnusan*” ([irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi 44](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/08/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-44/)), listened to [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)’s lamentations. He looked at the pitiable state of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), listened to the latter’s outpourings of his frustrations and thought. Without able to tolerate further, [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) thought that he should go to paramapadham where the knowledgeable people go, be one with the nithyasUris there, thereby making him one with them. [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) did not want to stop there and wanted [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) to get the eternal gift of doing service to them forever. Realizing this desire of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) thought that he had indeed got to paramapadham and became ecstatic because of his father [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s desire towards him. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), now was very confident of his destination as they say “*pERu thappAdhu enRu thuNindhu irukaiyum* ([mummukshupadi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/), dhvaya prakaraNam \#1) and starts to describe the journey of a soul that transcends this universe and goes to paramapadham.

**pAsuram**

*pOm vazhiyaith tharum ennum inbam ellAm*  
*pusiththu vazhipOy amudha virasaiyARRil*  
*nAm mUzhgi malamaRRuth theLivisumbai*  
*naNNi nalam thigazhmEni thannaip peRRu*  
*thAm amarar vandhu edhir koNdu alankarithu*  
*saRkarippa mAmaNi maNdapaththuch chenRu*  
*mAmalarAL kOn madiyil vaiththu ugakkum*  
*vAzhvu namakku ethirAsan aruLum vAzvhE **!!!***

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-20-august-19-2016)



**Word-by-Word Meanings:**

vAzhvu – The fortune  
aruLum vAzvhE – blessed by  
ethirAsan – emperumAnAr  
namakku – for us (is as follows)  
pOm vazhiyai – (when the soul departs the body), it proceeds in a path called as “archirAdhi mArgam” that serves as the way to the uninterrupted ethereal bliss in paramapadham  
tharum – The soul get this path  
ennum – and consequently  
pusiththu – enjoys  
inbam ellAm – all the happiness  
vazhipOy – as it traverses the “archirAdhi mArgam” path.  
nAm mUzhgi – (Later), the soul gets a holy dip  
amudha virasaiyARRil – in the river known as “virajA”  
malamaRRuth – and get rids of all the impurities caused due to nature.  
naNNi – (After this) it reaches  
theLivisumbai – the impeccable and faultless paramapadham  
nalam thigazhmEni thannaip peRRu – to get a body that is devoid any earthly natural attributes, one that is very pure and more importantly one that exhibits and radiates the true nature of the soul.  
thAm amarar – the nithyasUris  
vandhu – come,  
edhir koNdu – greet,  
alankariththu – decorate  
saRkarippa – and honor the soul which is now in a new unearthly body that  
mAmaNi maNtapathu chenRu – goes to the mandapam called “thirumAmaNi mandapam” and sees  
mAmalarAL kOn – [Sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) who is also known as “sriyapathi”, “vaikuntanAthan” and one who is the consort of periya pirAtti.  
madiyil vaiththu ugakkum – [Sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) will keep us in the lap, go ecstatic by happily feeling and smelling us (this fortune is only because of Sri rAmAnuja’s grace and nothing else).

**Simple Translation:**

In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) celebrates the grace of emperumAnAr who is the only one capable of liberating a soul from the bondage and ensuring that it is where it should be , i.e., paramapadham. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) describes joyfully, the wonderful journey the soul undergoes when it starts from this earth and reaches the ulterior destination in paramapadham. He describes how nithyasUris greet and honor this departed soul, which is welcomed by [Sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) who instantly become ecstatic.

**Explanation:**

As per [nammAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/)’s words “pOm vazhiyaith tharum nangaL ([thiruvAimozhi 3](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/thiruvaimozhi-3rd-centum/).9.3), the liberated soul departs from a body and traverses through the path known as “archirAdhi mArgam” that eventually leads to paramapadham. It enjoys all the luxuries along the way in its journey to paramapadham. Since the destination is ulterior and the most fascinating, the path that leads there has to be commensurate to that. Hence the soul that journeys in this path is being celebrated at the highest pedestal. The soul is being led by the lord as HE led “*kaLvan kol pirAtti*” (it is the name [parakAla nAyaki (feminine mood of thirumangai AzhwAr)](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/), specifically in periya thirumozhi 3.7). The soul gets a holy dip in the famous river called “virajA” as described by the phrase “virajAmAm amruthakArAm mAm prApyamahAnadhIm”. The soul gets a dip in this river, thereby cleansing its impurities and ill fates accrued over eons. After this, it gets a divine body that is devoid of any earthly natural qualities. This body is a one that radiates with the true nature of a soul that is nothing but being subservient to its eternal master [Sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). This person is now celebrated by nithyasUrIs as they meet, greet, honor and decorate him. They take him to a mandapam called “thirumAmaNi mandapam”. There, he meets [Sriya:pathi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/), who is known as SrivaikuNtanAthan. HE accepts the liberated person, hugs him and happily lifts him and smells his head (like a father would smell the child’s head) and goes ecstatic. This rare fortune to people like us who has interest in going to paramapadham, is an example of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s extreme compassion towards us because of which he grants us with this highest wealth.


## Arththi Prabandham – २१
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-20/)

[![ramanujar-srisailesa-mamunigal](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/ramanujar-srisailesa-mamunigal.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/ramanujar-srisailesa-mamunigal.jpg)

**Introduction:**

In this pAsuram [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is talking to his heart. We need to imagine figuratively that [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)’s heart is asking him a question. The question is that “Oh [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)! in the earlier pAsuram, you visually described the path to the spiritual abode known as paramapadham. Not stopping with that, you even described the unison between a soul and [Sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). This opportunity is extremely rare even to those who are well read and knowledgeable. But you talked about this opportunity as if you experienced it literally. What made you so confident and so fearless all of a sudden? Are you not afraid anymore?” [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) replied to this question that his heart posed him. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) tells his heart “Oh my dear heart! Do not fear anymore! The knowledge that I have is all given by the causeless mercy of my guru [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/). With that knowledge, I have come to the conclusion that only his ([thiruvAimozhip piLLai’s](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)) grace is the big ticket to liberation. Seeing this state of me, [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) would be so pleased and happy that he will do the required tasks automatically. Hence, I do not have any fear. So you too, do not have any fear anymore”.

**pAsuram:**

*thirumalai AzhvAr thiruvAimozhip piLLai sIraruLAl*  
*tharum madhi koNdavar thammai uththArakarAga eNNi*  
*iru manamE! avarkkAi ethirAsar emaik kadugap*  
*paramapadham thanil yERRuvAr enna bayam namakkE!!!*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-21)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings:**

[thirumalai AzhvAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) – The one who has the name “[SriSailESar](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)”  
[thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) – is none other than [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/).  
sIraruLAl – Out of his causeless mercy, he  
tharum – blessed me with  
madhi – his divine knowledge.  
manamE! – Hey my dear heart!  
koNdu – Using that knowledge as the means,  
iru – Please be  
eNNi – in the steadfast belief that  
avar thammai – thiruvAimozhippiLLai, the great one who helped to such an extent,  
uththArakarAga – is the one who will liberate from the shackles of this worldly bondage.  
ethirAsar – [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/),  
avarkkAi – for the sake of my AchAryan [thiruvAimozhippiLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/),  
yERRuvAr – will send  
emai – me, who stands by the rule “svAchArya abhimAnamE uththArakam” (the goodwill that a guru has on his sishyAs is the only saving grace for a sishyAs)  
kaduga – very soon  
paramapadham thanil – to paramapadham  
enna bayam namakkE!!! – Hey my heart! Hence why should we fear!!! There is no need to fear (One can sleep with hands on their chest and happily sleep thereupon)

**Simple Translation:**  
[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) tells his heart to have no fear for emperumAnAr will protect him. The reason emperumAnAr will surely protect and escalate him to paramapadham is because of the love and compassion that [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)‘s direct AchArya thiruvAimozhip piLLai has on him ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) learnt that the blessings that a guru showers on a persons and the subsequent compassion that he shows on him (Sishyas) alone would make emperumAnAr to expedite things for him.

**Explanation:**  
[thirumalai AzhvAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) was the original name. Later, because of his deep interest and knowledge in [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), he came to be famously known as “[thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)”. He was being known with his association towards [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/). That name stuck on to him and served as the most easy identification trait for him. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that such a great AchArya “[thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/), out of his causeless mercy, showered upon him the choicest blessings and the knowledge about the highest. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) was the recipient of all his knowledge. With that knowledge as the means, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) tells to his heart “Oh my dear heart! Please remember that the great [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) has granted us the knowledge. The use of such knowledge is for us to realize that it is he who is going to liberate us from the shackles of this earthly bondage. So my dear heart, I want you to be steadfast in that belief. If we can be steadfast in this belief, [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) will look at us and appreciate the state in which we are. Then, he will think about our AchAryan, and for his sake, will make sure that we go to paramapadham as soon as possible, as per the phrase “*ERRarum vaikuntham* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 7.6.10)”. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) continues towards his heart “So, you do not have to fear for anything, as they say “*manamE naiyal mEvudharkkE* ([irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) 98). One can sleep with their hands placed over their chest and sleep happily, for [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) will guarantee the ticket to paramapadham”.


## Arththi prabandham – २२
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/08/arththi-prabandham-21/)

[![thirukkudanthai_aravamudhazhvar_divine_feet](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/thirukkudanthai_aravamudhazhvar_divine_feet.png)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/thirukkudanthai_aravamudhazhvar_divine_feet.png)

**Introduction**

In the [earlier pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-21/), [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) used the phrase “*enna bhayam namakkE*” to mean that he does not have any more fear. In this pAsuram, he goes ahead and says that owing to his AchAryan [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)’s causeless blessings on him, [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) will take pride about him. This will help him in transgressing the big ocean called samAara (earthly bondage) and ascertain that he reaches the lotus feet of [sriman nArAyaNan.](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)

**pAsuram 22:**

*thIdhaRRa gyANam thiruvAimozhippillai sIraruLAl*  
*yEdhaththai mARRum ethirAsar than abhimAnamennum*  
*pOdhaththai yERip pavamAm puNaridhanaik kadandhu*  
*kOdhaRRa mAdhavan pAdhakkaraiyai kuRuguvanE!!!*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-22)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings:**

*thIdhaRRa* – The one without any fault  
*gyAna* – And complete knowledge of the true nature of a soul  
*[thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)* – Is known as “thiruvAimozhip piLLai” here, through his connection to [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/). thiruvAimozhi is the divine work by nammAzhvAr, who is the poet of SrIman nArAyaNan  
*sIraruLAl* – (He) blesses me causelessly  
*yEdhathai mARRum* – so that my faults like lust and desire are obliterated  
*ethirAsar tham* – His ([thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)) blessings will help me be in the good graces of rAmAnuja so that I can be assured of a ticket to board the  
*pOdhaththai yERip* – Unfaltering ship similar to “vishNu pOtham” or vishNu’s ship is the one  
*pavamAm puNaridhanaik kadandhu* – that helps travel the big ocean called samsAram  
*kuRuguvanE!* – And certainly attain  
*kOdhaRRa mAdhavan pAdhakkarayai* – the lotus feet of Sriya:pathi SrIman nArAyaNan. the lotus feet is described as “*viNNOr pirAnAr mAsil malaradikkIzh*”, “*thuyaraRu sudaradi*”, “one that is diametrically opposite of faults and that which dazzles brilliantly always  
kuRuguvanE!!!- will attain it

**Simple Translation:**

In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)says that he reaching the lotus feet of SrIman nArAyaNa is definite because he is going to be liberated from the earthly bondages with the aid of a ship that is similar to “*vishNu pOtham*”. This is certain because [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that Sri rAmAnuja would help him in getting him aboard the ship. The fact that [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) would help him in this way is ascertained because of the choicest blessings of his AchAryan , the impeccable [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/).

**Explanation:**

The commentator goes ahead and explains the greatness of [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/). He is someone who is devoid of faults associated with doing activities of any kind not attributed to [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), as expounded by the phrase, “*thath gyANam agyANamathOnyadhuktham*”, “*vidhyAnyAsilapanaipuNam*”. He does not sway even a little towards mundane matters as his mind and energy is always towards the spouse of [SrI mahAlakshmi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/), namely [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) (“*thAmaraiyAL kELvanayE nOkkum uNarvu*”, [mudhal thiruvandhAdhi 67](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/)).
His devotion towards[SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) stretches out to the extent in which he regards the devotees of[SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) as his master. He does pay any heed towards other scriptures except those related to [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). In particular, he dwells deep in the divine thiruvAimozhi and its esoteric purports so much that he was started to know in this world as “[thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)”. His love for thiruvAimozhi was so profound that people started to identify him with the work “thiruvAimozhi”. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is a Sishya of such a glorious AchArya in [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that his AchAryan’s blessings will ensure that he gets in the shade of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who would like him very much. [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is described as “kAmAdhidhOshaharam ([yathirAja vimshathi 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/08/yathiraja-vimsathi-1/))”.
maNavALa mAmunigaL continues that the connection with [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) would help him get liberated the samsAram (earthly bondage) using a srivaishNava ship that is similar to “vishNu pOtham”, that is often described as “idhamhi vaishNavam pOtham samyakAsthE bhavArNavE” or the “one that ensures that a person reaches the lotus feet of [sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) without any trouble”. The samsAra sAgaram is described in our scriptures as a scary ocean that is replete with dangers lurking everywhere, as per the phrase “*samsAra sAgaram ghOram anantha klEsa bhAjanam”* (jithanthE sthOthram 4). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that the ship will take him to the lotus feet of [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). HIS lotus feet, as described by “*viNNOrpirAnAr malaradikIzh* ([thiruviruththam](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) 54)” and “*thuyar aRu sudaradi”* ([thiruvAimozhi 1.1.1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-1-1-uyarvara/)) are something that is worshipped by the nithyasUris and are the one that remove all the ignorance and sufferings of a person. They are completely devoid of any faults and is diametrically opposite of blemishes, as described by “*hEya prathyanIkam*”. In addition to it, the lotus feet dazzled brilliantly with divine glow and is something that does not need the help of someone or something else to protect a person. Such impeccable lotus feet of[SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) is my destination. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that he reaching it is definite.

The term “kOdhaRRa” that means impeccable and would qualify the lotus feet.
