On the other side, since the phrase is “kOdhaRRa mAdhavan”, this can also be taken to mean “impeccable or faultless mAdhavan”. The fault that is being alluded here is the fault of sriman nArAyaNan when HE is alone, without HIS divine consort, who is known as “[pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/)”. This is being resonated by thiruvadi (hanumAn) when he said, “rAmasyalOkathraya nAyakasya sripAdhakUlam manasAjakAma”. The same fact is being told by nammAzhvAr in “mAnei nOkki madavALai mArbil koNdAi mAdhavA” and culminates in “un thEnE malarum thirupAdham vinayEn sErumAru nI aruLAi ([thiruvAimozhi 1.5](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/08/thiruvaimozhi-1-5-valavezh/).5)”. Hence, the fault (kOdhu) would surface only when [sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) is seen without [pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/) (thiruvillAdha kOdhu aRRavan). Hence it goes to prove that only [sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) with [pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/) is the final destination, as only HE is the one without any fault.


## Arththi prabandham – २३
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/09/arththi-prabandham-22/)

[![paramapadhanathan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/paramapadhanathan.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/paramapadhanathan.jpg)

**Introduction**

In the last two pAsurams, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)described about the choices blessings of his own AchAryan in [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and paramAchAryan emperumAnAr. Against the backdrop of the mercy of these two, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is very sure that their blessings will not fail, ensuring hisascent to paramapadham and enjoy the Lord there. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) expresses his desire to go there as soon as possible to enjoy the Lord who resides in the “dhivyasthAna maNdapam” (the divine altar) and is seated in the “dhivya simhAsaNam” (the divine throne of the Lord).

**pAsuram**

*adiyArgaL kuzhAngaL azhagOlakkam irukka*  
*AnanthamayamAna mAmaNi mandapaththu*  
*padiyAdhumil padukkaiyAy irukkum ananthan*  
*paNamAmaNigaL thammin oLi maNdalaththil idaiyil*  
*vadivArum mAmalarAL valavarugu maRRai*  
*maNmagaLum AymagaLum idavarugum irukka*  
*naduvAga vIRRirukkum nAraNanaik kaduga*  
*nAn anubhavikkum vagai nalgu en ethirAsA!!!*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-23)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings:**

en ethirAsA – Oh! yathirAja! my master! The leader of yathis!!!  
kaduga – (You should) soon  
nalgu – shower your blessings on  
nAn – me  
anubhavikkum vagai – to enjoy  
nAraNanai – SrIvaikuNtanAthan  
naduvAga vIRRirukkum – the one who is seated in the middle, like a lotus in between sheaths of lightning, one who is like a dark hued rain bearing clouds, the one who is seated in between them (divine consorts) to rule over the worlds  
vadivArum mAmalarAL – The consorts are periya pirAttiyAr, the one who is known for her unparalleled beauty and her soft nature as revealed by “vaidvAy nin valamArbinil vAzhginRa mangai ([thirupallAndu 2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu-2-adiyomodum/))”  
valavarugu – on the right side  
maRRai manmagaLum AymagaLum – and bhUmip pirAtti and neeLA dhEvi who are  
idavarugum irukka – on the left side.  
adiyArgaL kuzhAngaL – In addition to them, there is a beautiful collection of nithyasUris and mukthas (nithyasUris including the likes of ananthan, garudan, vishwaksEnar etc; mukthas including the likes of [parAnkusa](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) and [parakAla](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/)). This collection looks like a beautiful collection of pearl and gems  
azhagOlakkam irukka – that are beautifully lined  
AnandhamayamAna mAmaNi mandapaththu – in the altar that beams with infinite happiness, that is known as “thirumAmaNi maNdapam”  
paNamAmaNigaL thammin oLi maNdalaththil idaiyil – amidst the resplendent glow that radiates from the heads of the  
padiyAdhumil – one that is beyond any comparison  
padukkaiyAi irukkum – ananthan, the one that serves as the divine bed (of SrIman nArAyaNan)  
ananthan – and is known by the name of “ananthAzhvAn”

**Simple Translation**

In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) asks [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) to bless him so that he can go to paramapadham and enjoy srivaikuNtanAthan as soon as possible without any delay. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) describes SrIvaikuNtanAthan as the one who is seated amidst his divine consorts of periya pirAtti, bhUmi dhEvi and nIlA dhEvi in the thirumAmaNi maNtapam amidst the glorious line of nithyasUris including ananthan, garudan, [vishwaksEnar](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/18/senai-mudhaliar/) as well as mukthAthmAs that includes [AzhvArs](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/azhwars/) and [AchAryAs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/).

**Explanation**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)L says, “Oh! My master! The leader of yathIs (sanyAsis)!!! The nithyasUris are the mukthAs are all beautifully lined up as they say “*adiyArgaL kuzhAngaL* ([thiruvAimozhi 2.3.10](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/02/thiruvaimozhi-2-3-unil-vazh/))” and “mAmaNi maNtapathu anthamil pErinbaththadiyAr ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.9.11)”. The nithyasUris include the likes of anantha, garuda, [vishwaksEnar](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/18/senai-mudhaliar/) etc., whereas the mukthas include the likes of [parAnkusa](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/18/nammazhwar/), [parkAla](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) and yathivarAdhigal. These devotees are beautifully lined up that it looks like a beautiful garland of pearls and gems decked together. They are lined before the resplendent, that which radiates infinite happiness and that which is known by the name of “thirumAmaNi maNdapam” as per “AnandhamayAya maNdapa rathnAya nama:”. In this maNdapam is the great serpent bed called “ananthan” who is synonymous with “eternal service to the Lord” and one who is unparalleled in softness and coolness. “ananthan” is described in numerous places including, “Ayiram painthalai ananthan ([periyAzhvAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/01/20/periyazhwar/) thirumozhi 4.3.10)”, “siRappudaiya paNangaL misaichchezhumaNigaL vitterikkum ([periyAzhvAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/01/20/periyazhwar/) thirumozhi 4.9.7)”, and “dheyvachchudar naduvuL ([periya thirumadal](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) 1)”.[periya pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/) is someone who is identified with her quality of beauty and soft nature as seen in the phrases like “[vadivAy nin vala mArbinil vAzhginRa mangai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu-2-adiyomodum/) (thiruppallANdu 2) and “vadikkOla vAL nedunkaN ([iraNdAm thiruvandhAdhi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) 82)”. She is seen at the right hand side of [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). On HIS left side are the bhUmi pirAtti and nIlA dhEvi who are the shadows of [periya pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/). Sriman nArAyaNan is seen between these three pirAttis like a a lotus like dark rain bearing cloud is seen with three beaming streaks of lightning. HE is known as [SrIvaikuNtanAthan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) who is described as “vAzhpugazh nAraNan ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.9.1)”, who is seated there to rule over the worlds (“vIRRindhu yEzhulagam thanikkOl sella ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 4.5.1)”. Oh! My master ethirAsA!!! Please shower me with your choicest blessings for me to immediately enjoy such a [SrIvaikuNtanAthan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)”.


## Arththi Prabandham – २४
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/09/arththi-prabandham-23/)

[![paramapadham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/09/paramapadham.jpeg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/09/paramapadham.jpeg)

**Introduction:** In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) describes the events from the time when the mortal coil is shed to the extreme fortune of being amidst the glorious [AchAryas](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/full-list).

**pAsuram**

*indha udal vittu iravimaNdalaththUdu yEgi*  
*ivvaNdam kazhiththu idaiyil AvaraNamEzh pOy*  
*anthamil pAzh kadandhu azhagAr virasaithanil kuLiththu angu*  
*amAnavanAl oLi koNda sOdhiyum peRRu amarar*  
*vandhu edhirkoNdu alankariththu vAzhththi vazhinadaththa*  
*vaikuntham pukku maNimaNdapaththuch chenRu*  
*nam thirumAladiyArgaL kuzhAngaLudan kUdum*  
*nAL enakkuk kurugum vagai nalgu en ethirAsA*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-24)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings**

en ethirAsA – Oh! ethirAsA! my master! The leader of yathis!!!  
nalgu – Please bless  
enakku – me  
kurugum vagai – that the days between today and that opportune day, shrinks rapidly.  
kUdum nAL – That opportune day is the day when I join  
nam thirumAladiyArgaL – our masters (who are actually servants of Sriya:pathi SrIman nArAyaNan) who are known as ‘nithyasUris’  
kuzhAngaLudan – and be one in their group.  
indha udal – (This happens after) this mortal body of mine that is replete with impurities  
vittu – discards itself  
iravimaNdalaththUdu yEgi – and transgresses the solar orbit and  
kazhiththu – transgresses  
ivvaNdam – this universe  
idaiyil – that is in between  
AvaraNamEzh pOy – (after which) it transgresses the seven oceans  
pAzh kadandhu – only to continue transgressing the “mUla prakruthi”  
anthamil – that is described as never ending or abysmal.  
azhagAr – Finally, it reaches the very beautiful  
virasaithanil – river called “vrajA”  
kuLiththu – takes a holy bath  
angu – there  
amAnavanAl – and gets lifted by the touch of a person known as “amAnavan”  
oLi koNda sOdhiyum peRRu – and as a result, get a divine body that oozes with resplendence.  
amarar vandhu edhirkoNdu – Thereupon, the nithyasUris come and greet  
alankariththu – decorate  
vAzhthi – praise  
vazhinadaththa – and lead me (in the new body) in  
vaikuntham pukku – the path towards SrIvaikuntham  
maNimaNdapaththuch chenRu – and reach the altar known as “thirumAmaNi maNdapam”

**Simple Translation:**  
In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)asks [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) to bless him that the days between now and the day of joining the nithyasUri ranks, shrink rapidly. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) goes ahead and describes the journey after the mortal body falls. The soul transgresses multiple locations including the solar orbit, universe, seven oceans and finally reach the river that is known as “vrajA”. In that holy river, it takes a bath upon which a person known as “amAnavan” lifts and the soul gets a new resplendent body thereupon. The nithyasUris come, greet, decorate and usher him towards thirumAmaNi maNdapam where Sriya:pathi SrIman nArAyaNan is seated. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)requests that the duration between now and his reaching the eternal abode of nithyasUris diminish quickly.

**Explanation:**  
[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)says, “Oh! My master! The leader of yathIs (sanyAsis)!!! This mortal body of mine is something that is replete with impurities as they say “*immAyavAkkai* (thiruvAimozhi 10.7.3)”. This body is not something to be desired and hence should completely be destroyed as per the phrase “manga ottu ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)10.7.9)”. After this the soul crosses multiple worlds and universes starting from the solar orbit as described by the phrase “*mannum kadum kadhirOn maNdalaththin nannaduvuL* ([periya thirumadal](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) 16)”. After this, it transgresses the worlds that are occupied by people who are known as “AdhivAhikas”. Subsequently, it crosses the world that measures 1 crore yOjanAs and are inhabitated by dhEvas , as revealed by the phrase “*imayOrvAzh thanimuttai kOttai* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 4.9.8)”. After this, it transgresses the seven oceans to reach the neven ending “mUla prakruthi” that is described as “*mudivil perumpAzh* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)10.10.10)”. After crossing these, the soul reaches the most beautiful river called “vrajA”. It takes a holy bath in it after which a person who is known by the name of “[amAnavan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/02/upadhesa-raththina-malai-74-and-conclusion/)” comes and gives his hand to help come out from vrajA river. When this touch happens, the soul gets a new body that oozes with bright resplendence as per the phrase “*oLikkoNda sOdhiyumAi* ([thiruvAimozhi 2.3.10)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/02/thiruvaimozhi-2-3-unil-vazh/))” and that which is often described as “*panchOpanishath mayam*” (made of five spiritual elements). After this, the nithyaSuris come and greet the soul (in the new body) as per “mudiyudai vAnavar muRaimuRai edhirkoLLa ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)10.9.8). They decorate him, praise him and usher him to the holy place known as “SrIvaikuNtam”. They take him until the altar that is famously known as “thirumAmaNi maNtapam”, along which there are numerous devotees”. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) asks [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), “As they say “*adiyArgaL kuzhAngaLudan kUduvadhu yeNrukolO* ([thiruvAimozhi 2.3.10)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/02/thiruvaimozhi-2-3-unil-vazh/)” and “*mathdhEvathai: parijanaisthava sankishUya:*”, when will I get a chance to be amidst those great devotees? Those devotees are our masters. They are the servants of Sriya:pathi [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and their proof of their very existence is established through their doing kainkaryam to HIM. Hey [ethirAsA](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! Please bless me that the day between today and that day when the aforementioned list of things happen, actually shrink.


## Arththi Prabandham – २५
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/09/arththi-prabandham-24/)

[![EmperumAnar_thirukoshtiyur](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/EmperumAnar_thirukoshtiyur.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/EmperumAnar_thirukoshtiyur.jpg)

**Introduction**

In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) raises an imaginary question. He believesthat Sri rAmAnuja might have had this as a question onhis mind and subsequently [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) tries to answer him in this pAsuram. The question / assumption is as follows. [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) asked maNavALa mAmunigaL, “hey [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)!!! You have not taken account of the sins that you have accrued. Yet you yearned for \[the opportunity to serve\]. What should I do now in this regard? Please tell me”. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) replies, “hey! [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! The time between the day when you took me to your fold and today, you have patiently watched my sins. You have also ensured me of paramapadham, for which I did not have any eligibility. Now, you should not delay it further and should grant me mOksham immediately”.

**pAsuram 25**

*enRu nirEthukamAga ennai abhimAniththu*  
*yAnum adhaRindhu unakkEyAyirukkum vagai seydhAi*  
*anRu mudhal inRaLavum anavaratham pizhaiyE*  
*aduththaduththuch cheyvadhu anuthavippadhu inichcheyyEn*  
*enRu unnai vandhu irappadhAm en kodumai kaNdum*  
*igazhAdhE iravupagal adimai koNdu pOndhAy*  
*inRu thirunAdum enakku aruLa eNNuginRAy*  
*inik kadugach cheidharuLavENdum ethirAsA!!!*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-25)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings**

[ethirAsA](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) – Oh! [ethirAsA](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! my master! The leader of yathis!!!  
enRu – From the day  
nirEthukamAga – (when you) without any reason  
ennai – developed a thought towards me  
abhimAniththu – that “I ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) am yours”  
yAnum – I, too  
adhaRindhu – knew about it  
unakkE – (and served) you and you only  
Ayirukkum – (and made myself) a thing that is reserved for you only and to no one else  
seydhAy – You did this. Did’nt you?  
vagai – (for me to have this regard for you) this way.  
anRu mudhal – From that day  
inRaLavum – till now  
anavaratham – (I am) always  
aduththaduththu – incessantly  
cheivadhu – committing  
pizhaiyE – only sins  
anuthavippadhu – and am instantly repenting for those sins that  
ini – hereafter  
cheyyEn enRu – I should not commit (those sins)  
unnai vandhu irappadhAm – and I come to you and plead you for support.  
en kodumai kaNdum – You, even after you seeing my attorcious sins  
igazhAdhE – have never dismissed / hated me for that  
adimai koNdu pOndhAy – (Instead) you accepted my kainkaryam at your lotus feet  
iravupagal – day and night.  
inRu – (not stopping with that) today  
eNNuginRAy – you are thinking of  
aruLa – blessing  
enakku – me  
thirunAdum – with paramapadham  
inik kaduga – so, quickly  
cheidhu aruLavENdum – bless me with that.

**Simple Translation**

In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) asks [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) to quickly grant him the ticket to paramapadham. He says that right from the day when [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) took him to his lotus feet with the thought that “[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)is mine” till today, he is incessantly committing innumerable sins. Just moments after committing those sins, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that he would repent very much for doing it but that would never stop him from doing it again. This has been the case for a long time and all these days, Sri rAmAnuja did not look at the sinful side of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), nor did he hate him for doing that. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that instead he made sure that he got uninterrupted service at his lotus feet day in and day out. Today, [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) was even contemplating on blessing [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) with the paramapdham. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) asks [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), if that is the case, what is the reason for the delay and requests him to bless immediately.

**Explanation**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)says, “Oh! The leader of yathIs (sanyAsis)!!! You have blessed this soul with your thought that “this soul is mine”. You have done so without any reason for it. I knew about it and thanks to your blessings, I became an entity reserved exclusively for you and for no one else. From that very day till today when I seek your lotus feet, I have continued to incessantly commit nothing but sins. I repent immediately and plead to you for support. You did not dismiss me or hate me for doing sins. On the contrary, you have giftedme with uninterrupted service to you , at your lotus feet, day in and day out. Not stopping with that, today you were even thinking of granting me paramapdham, the place reserved for highly deserving people. You were thinking to offer me a ticket to paramapdham, a place to which I am completely ineligible to go to. Having had this very thought, [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), what is the reason for your delay? I request you to bless me immediately”.


## Arththi prabandham – २६
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/09/arththi-prabandham-25/)

[![ramanuja_vaibhavam_8_per](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/ramanuja_vaibhavam_8_per.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/ramanuja_vaibhavam_8_per.jpg)

**Introduction**

In this pAsuram[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), who knows the heart of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) and speaks on his behalf. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) knows what [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is thinking and pours it in this pAsuram. He concludes with the request to [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) about quickly granting him the ascendancy to paramapadham. [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is thinking “This person [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) has committed lots of sins right from the day he came to me. If not for me, will there be any other person who can protect him in spite of his huge repository of sins? There might not be any one and so we should protect him”. This thought of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is what [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)is reproducing in this pAsuram as if it is coming from his own heart. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), in continuation says who other than [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) could protect him, being the only refuge for all people without any shelterwhatsoever. Can the ever compassionate people that include the likes of [periya perumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) protect me? [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that it was [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who kindledthe desire to go to the ultimate destination of paramapdham. Hence, he requests that it has to be [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who needs to ensure that he reaches there. In addition to it, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says that it is [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s thought that he ought to protect him from those innumerable sins that he commits daily. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)believes that itis not [periya perumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) etc who are trying to protect [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), instead it is [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is pining to save him from all sorts of sins and no one else”.

**pAsuram 26**

thennarangarkkAmO? dhEviyargatkAmO?  
sEnaiyarkOn mudhalAna sUriyargatkAmO?  
manniyasIr mARan aruLmAri thamakkAmO?  
maRRUm uLLa dhEsigargaL thangaLukkumAmO?  
ennudaiya pizhai poRukka yAvarukku mudiyum?  
ethirAsA unakku anRi yAn oruvarukku AgEn  
un aruLAl enakku ruchi thannaiyum uNdAkki  
oLivisumbil adiyEnai oruppaduththu viraindhE!!!

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-26)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings**

ethirAsA – Oh emperumAnArE!!!  
thennarangarkkAmO? (To forgive my sins) will periya perumAL be capable to do it? or  
dhEviyargatkAmO? – will the divine consorts including the likes of periya pirAtti be capable to do it? or  
sEnaiyarkOn mudhalAna sUriyargatkAmO? – will the nithyasUris starting from [sEnApathiyAzhvAn](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/18/senai-mudhaliar/) be capable to do it? or  
manniya sIr – the one, who, forever has the auspicious qualities of vAthsalyam etc towards devotees of the Lord  
mARan – and is known by the name of [nammAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/), would he be capable to do it? or  
aruLmAri thamakkAmO? – will [thirumangai AzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/) who showers compassion towards all chEthanas, be capable to do it? or  
maRRUm uLLa – will any other  
dhEsigargaL – AchAryas starting from nAthamunigaL,  
thangaLukkumAmO? – will they be able to do it?  
yAvarukku mudiyum? – Who can  
pizhai poRukka – forgive the sins  
ennudaiya – that I committed?  
yAn – I  
oruvarukku AgEn – will not be a servant to anyone else  
unakku anRi – except you.  
un aruLAl – With your grace, you  
ruchi thannaiyum uNdAkki – have instilled the desire in prApyam (paramapadham)  
enakku – in me  
oruppaduththu adiyEnai – (you) should make me reach the  
oLivisumbil – bright and resplendent paramapadham.  
E – (at the end of viraindhu) – is a suffix added for the sake of completion.

**Simple Translation**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) talks about the cream of cream people including the likes of periya perumAL, HIS divine consorts, nithyasUris, AzhvArs and other AchAryas except [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). He says that none of them has the means to protect him and thereby forgive his sins. Only [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) has the capability and compassion to do so. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)explains this thought of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), concluding by requesting [SrI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) to take him to paramapadham and be one among the people there.

**Explanation**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says “Oh! The leader of yathIs!!! Even the omnipotent Lord who knows everything without the help of anything or anyone, cannot fathom the sins that I have committed. Is there any one who is capable of forgiving my sins? Will the [periya perumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), who is described by the phrases, “dhOshAyadhyabhithasyasyAth” and “en adiyAr adhu seyyAr seydhArEl nanRu seydhAr ([periyAzhvAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/01/20/periyazhwar/) thirumozhi 4.9.2)” be able to forgive my sins? My sins will test even HIS patience. Will, the set of pirAttis starting from [periya pirAtti](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/), who is described as “nakaschin naparAdhyathi (srIrAmAyaNam)” and “*kimEthan nirdhOsha: ihajagathi* ([SrI guNa rathna kOsam](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/11/parasara-bhattar/))”, be able to patiently forgive my sins? Will, the nithyasUris, starting from the likes of [sEnApathiyAzhvAn](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/18/senai-mudhaliar/) etc. who have yearned and got the eternal service of[periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) and HIS [pirAttis](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/), be capable of forgiving my sins? All these nithyasUris are one and the same when it comes to doing eternal service to [perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) and [pirAtti](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/), as shown by “*asmAbhis thulyObhavathu*”. They are the people who talked about prapaththi in “*vishvaksEna samhithai*” and “*vihakEndhra samhithai*”. Will any of those nithyasUris, be able to forgive my sins? Will [nammAzhvAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/18/nammazhwar/), who, forever, is replete with auspicious qualities of vAthsalyam to devotees, and who stands by it as revealed by the phrase “[*payananRAgilum pAngallarAgilum seyal nanRAgaththiruthip paNikoLvAn*](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/02/kanninun-chiruth-thambu-10-payan-anragilum/) ([kaNNinun chiruth thAmbu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) 10)”, be capable of forgiving my sins”? Will [thirumangai AzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/), who showers his choicest blessings on all chEthanas (anything with consciousness), be capable of forgiving my sins? Will it be possible for all [krupAmAthra prasannAchAryas](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2015/12/simple-guide-to-srivaishnavam-acharya-sishya.html), who are recipients of AzhvAr’s blessings, starting from [nAdhamunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/), [yAmunamuni](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/01/alavandhar/) and the like, to forgive my sins? Except for you, [SrI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), who bears and forgives any sin patiently, will any one of the aforementioned elite people be able to forgive my sins at all? It is not at all possible for them to forgive my sins. Hence, going by the phrase that describe you as “[*nigarinRi ninRavennIsadhaikku nin aruLingaNanRip pugalonRumillai*](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/08/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-48/) ([rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) 48)”, you are verily the ocean of compassion and the one who forgives and protects everyone with the huge baggage of sins anyone may have. So, it is only appropriate for me to say that I belong to you and to no one else”.

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) continues, “It is because of your blessings that, the surrender unto your lotus feet, was possible. Likewise, after surrender, it is because of your blessings again that I got interest in reaching the ultimate destination (prApyam). I request you to take me to paramapdham that is described as “s*udaroLiyAi ninRa thannudaichOdhi* ([thiruvAimozhi 3](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/thiruvaimozhi-3rd-centum/).10.5)” and “*theLivisumbu* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 9.7.5)” and make me one among them there. Without making me an outcast from those people in paramapdham, as described by the phrase “anguRREn allEn ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 5.7.2)”, I request you to quickly give me ascendancy to paramapadham.
The word “unakkanRi” (except for you) can be connected with both “thennarangar…..ethirAsa” and “yAn oruvarukku AgEn”. (This would convey the meaning that except [SrI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) no one is capable of forgiving the sins committed by [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) and except [SrI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is not for anyone.

The reasons why the aforementioned elite league of people may not be able to completely tolerate, forgive and protect [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) from his sins is explained below. Lord [Sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) is someone who is characterized by the character called total independence without any cause (nirankusasvAthanthriyam). HE can be independent at any time that HE chooses and may punish a person for his sin, as revealed by “kshipAmi” and “nakshamAmi”. The set of [pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/)s are described by the phrases “kshAmA lakshmI bhrungIsakala karaNOnmAthanamadhu” and “thimir koNdAL oththu niRkkum ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 6.5.2)” mean that they may be overly absorbed with their Lord that they may be resemble a statue. They may not be in a situation to forgive my sins. When it comes to nithyasUris who are always in the eternal service to the Lord and HIS divine consorts (the set of [pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/)s), they would always care for any danger to the Lord and their divine consorts, even it is out of place or out of time. The nithyasUris might be in constant fear of any lurking danger for the Lord and their consorts, as described in “AngaravAram adhu kEttu azhalumizhum ([nAnmugan thiruvandhAdhi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) 10)”. Hence, they may not be able to protect / forgive the sins of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/). Next up are AzhvArs who always yearn for the kainkaryam at the lotus feet of the Lord and pirAttis. In doing so, they become ecstatic at times and forget themselves owing to their great bhakthi (devotion) to the Lord and His consorts. The AzhvArs are epitome of bhakthi as described by the phrases “sindhai kalangi thirumAL enRazhaippan ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 9.8.10)”, “unnaikANum avAvil vIzhndhu ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 5.7.2)”, “unnaikkANum Asai ennum kadalil vIzhndhu (periya thirumozhi 4.9.3)” and “bhakthi pAravashyaththAle prapannargaL AzvhArgaL ([SrI vachana bhUshaNam](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) 43)”. Hence, they may not be capable of forgiving me and my sins. Lastly, the group of mumukshUs (those who have the interest in attaining mOksham or paramapdham) are people who follows the code of conduct (the do’s and don’t’s) as long as they are in a body. Till their mortal coils falls on the ground, they are supposed to yearn about mOksham and supposed to be doing that at all time. Hence, they are not entitled this job of advising other people, forgiving others sins etc. However, [SrI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) is beyond these limitations of others when it comes to protecting someone from their sins. He is someone who, looks at the misfortune of samsAris, and protects them, even if it means to finish himself. He does not look at their knowledge or lack of it. He protects them and forgives all sorts of sins that one may have committed. In addition to doing this, he makes sure that he gets the character of singing mangaLAsAsaNam to the Lord as per “ALumALar engiRavanudaiya thanimai thIrumpadi ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.3.3)”. So he is the one who rectifies a person that were deemed as “cannot be reformed” as per the phrase “adhu thiruthalAvadhE ([periya thiruvandhAdhi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/18/nammazhwar/) 25)”. Eventually he ensures that that is person does eternal service at the Lord [srIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) who is described as “thirumagaL kElvan”. [thiruvarangaththu amudhanAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/amudhanar/) also sang about this in “maruL koNdiLaikkum namakku nenjE irAmAnusan seyyum sEmangaL maRRuLAr tharamO ([irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi
39](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/08/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-39/))” in this regard.


## Arththi prabandham – २७
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/09/arththi-prabandham-26/)

[![paramapadham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/paramapadham.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/paramapadham.jpg)

**Introduction:**

In the [earlier pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/09/arththi-prabandham-26/), [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) asked [SrI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) “*oLi visumbil adiyEnai oruppaduththu viraindhE*”. He requested [SrI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) to expedite the process of him going to paramapadham. [SrI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) also will give [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) as per the phrase “*vAnE tharuvAn enakkAy* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.8.5)”, after seeing the latter’s steadfast yearning in reaching paramapadham. With paramapadham assured, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) tells his heart about the dos and don’ts from this point on. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) starts by telling his heart to pay noattention towards the hurdles in this materialistic world. He continues to list the dos for his heart, with the undercurrent that his ascend to paramapadham, the ultimate destination, has been confirmed.

**pAsuram 27**

ivvulaginil ini onRum eNNAdhE nenjE  
iravupagal ethirAsar emakku inimEl aruLum  
avvulagai alarmagaLkOn angirukkum iruppai  
adiyArgaL kuzhAngaL thamai avargaL anubhavaththai  
ivvuyirum adhukku ittuppiRandhu izhandhu kidandhadhu  
ennum aththai enRum adhukku idaichuvarAy kidakkum  
vevvinaiyAl vandha udal vidum pozhudhai vittAl  
viLaIyum inbam thannai muRRum vidAmal irundhu eNNE!

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-27)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings:**

nenjE – hey! My heart!!!  
eNNAdhE – Do not think about  
onRum – anything  
ivvulaginil – about this world  
ini – from now.  
eNNE! – (Instead) think  
vidAmal irundhu – incessantly  
iravupagal – day and night  
avvulagai – about the celestial world (paramapadham) that  
ethirAsar – Sri rAmAnuja  
inimEl aruLum – will bestow in future  
emakku – for us  
alarmagaLkOn – (think about) the omnipotent, omniscient [Lord sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), who is the divine consort of [periya pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/), who is seated on a lotus flower  
irukkum iruppai – (Think about) HIS being at the divine majestic throne  
angu – out there in paramapadham.  
avargaL anubhavaththai – (Think about) being an object of enjoyment for  
kuzhAngaL thamai – the communities of  
adiyArgaL – nithyasUris.  
enRum – (Think about) at all times  
ennum aththai – that  
ittuppiRandhu – very well deserved yet  
izhandhu kidandhadhu – lost opportunity (of being an object of enjoyment to the nithyasUris)  
ivvuyirum – even this soul.  
adhukku idaichuvarAy kidakkum – (Think about) those that acts as obstacle  
vandha – caused by  
vevvinaiyAl – cruel sins (which in turn is caused by association with the body)  
udal vidum pozhudhai – (Think about) the time when the body falls  
adhukku – (Think about) the enjoyment that ensues  
vittAl – when the body falls  
viLaiyum – which eventually causes  
inbam thannai – eternal happiness  
muRRum – (think about) all these aforementioned list

**Simple Translation:**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) asks his heart to think about the glorious time that this soul is going to have in paramapadham. He says that this was blessed by [SrI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) who had earlier inculcated the interest in going to paramapadham. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) tells his heart to think about paramapadham, the divine couple of [Sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and [periya pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/), THEIR devotees, the opportunity of being an object of enjoyment to the devotees, the misfortune of the soul not able to attain it now, the hurdles that prevent the soul from being served as an object of enjoyment of the devotees, the sins that acts as an obstacle, the body that was the cause of the sins, the time when the body falls for one last time, the subsequent time when it is going to be in paramapdham thereafter.

**Explanation:**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) tells his heart “Hey! My heart! You are responsible for both, path to bondage as well as path to liberation from it (via paramapadham).” “*atha dhEhAvasAnEcha thyaktha sarvEdhAsbruha:*” is a saying that describes that this materialistic world is replete with things that are to be looked with disdain. These things that are collectively called as “*prakruthi prAkruthungaL*” are clearly something that are to be discarded completely without any trace of it. These things that are silly, ephemeral etc., are never to be considered as things to be adopted / approved in the first place.” [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) continues, “Hey! My heart! [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) had inculcated in me, the desire to reach paramapadham. Hence, from now, I am going to ask you to always think about the following list of things. To start with, think about the glorious celestial world, also known as “paramapdham” that [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is going to bestow us. Think about the [Lord Sriman nArAyaNan,](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) the divine consort of [periya pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/),and HIS majestic sitting posture in the throne there in paramapdham. [periya pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/) who looks like someone who is fragrance personified is seen seated in a lotus flower. She is with her consort [Lord sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) in the divine throne as described by the phrase “*ezhil malar mAdharum thAnum ivvEzhulagai inbam payakka inidhudan vIRRirundhu* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 7.10.1)”. Think about the glorious list of devotees (“*adiyAr kuzhAngaLai* ([thiruvAimozhi 2.3.10](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/02/thiruvaimozhi-2-3-unil-vazh/))”, who are engaged in eternal service to the divine couple (Lord [Sriman nArAyAnan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and [periya pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/)). Think about the enjoyment that you will derive upon seeing them enjoy you. Think about the misfortune now of not being regarded as an object of enjoyment by those devotees, though you (the soul) is qualified for that in every sense. Think about this great loss. Think about the hurdles that caused this great loss (of being enjoyed by the devotees) in the first place. Think about the body that is the biggest hurdle in achieving that. Think about the innumerable sins that served as the cause for the body in the first place as revealed by *“pollA ozhukkum azhukkudambum* ([thiruvirutham](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) 1)”. Think about the time when this body falls for one last time. Think about the subsequent wonderful time that the soul is going to be forever once this mortal coil falls. Think about all these things day and night. These are the things that are in line with “things to think of” for the soul. Think about these things incessantly day in and day out”. The phrase “*ivvulagil ini onRum eNNAdhE*” in this pAsuram is in line with what [nammAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) mentioned in his [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) pAsuram “*maruL ozhi nI* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.6.1)”. Both talk about the significance of archAvathAram.


## Arththi Prabandham – २८
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/10/arththi-prabandham-27/)

[![srivaishna-guruparamparai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srivaishna-guruparamparai.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srivaishna-guruparamparai.jpg)

**Introduction:**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://chameleon.tsi.lan/DevHelp/ResponsePage/5413) celebrates the choicest blessings of [SrI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) towards him, that made him to do something that he had never paid any attention whatsoever. In his earlier life, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://chameleon.tsi.lan/DevHelp/ResponsePage/5413) had done all wise activities yet he did not have the interest in going to paramapadham. Only after [SrI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) graced him and instigated the desire to reach paramapadham, he focused on ascending to paramapadham. Thus, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://chameleon.tsi.lan/DevHelp/ResponsePage/5413) praises this golden blessing of[SrI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) in this pAsuram.

**pAsuram:**

*paNdu palavAriyarum pArulagOruyyap*  
*parivudanE seydharuLum palkalaigaL thammaik*  
*kaNdadhellAm ezhudhi avai kaRRirundhum piRarkkuk*  
*kAdhaludan kaRpiththum kAlaththaik kazhithEn*  
*puNdarIgai kELvanuRai ponnulagu thannil*  
*pOga ninaivu onRuminRip poRundhi ingE irundhEn*  
*eNdisaiyum yEththum ethirAsan aruLAle*  
*ezhil visumbEyanRi ippOdhen manam eNNAdhE!!!*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-28)

  
**Word-by-Word Meanings:**

paNdu – earlier  
kAlaththaik kazhithEn – I spent my life by  
kAdhaludan – lovingly  
kaRpiththum – propagating/educating  
piRarkku – to other people  
avai kaRRirundhum – what I learned from my guru  
kaNdadhellAm – (that includes) all the knowledge in the books that I saw  
ezhudhi – wrote about which I learned  
palkalaigaL thammai – Those multitude of books  
seydharuLum – were magnanimously given by  
palavAriyarum – those gurus who have always contemplated and stood by tenets concerning the “upliftment and betterment of the soul”  
parivudanE – and gave (those books) with compassion towards these chEthanas so that  
pArulagOruyyap – the chEthanas (sentient beings) in this world to get uplifted (liberated from bondage).  
poRundhi ingE irundhEn – I was staying happily in this vibhUthi  
pOga ninaivu onRuminRi – without having any iota of inclination to go to  
ponnulagu thannil – paramapadham that is known as “nithya vibhUthi”  
uRai – which is the dwelling place of  
puNdarIgai kELvan – [sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), who is the divine consort of [periya pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/) who is seated on a lotus flower.  
ippOdhen manam eNNAdhE – (But now) my heart will not think about anything else  
ezhil visumbEyanRi – except the resplendent paramapadham.  
ethirAsan aruLAle – (This is due to) [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)‘s blessings.  
eNdisaiyum yEththum – He is someone whose glories are being praised by people in all eight directions

**Simple Translation:**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://chameleon.tsi.lan/DevHelp/ResponsePage/5413) talks about how he used to spend his life earlier. He used to read the books that were given to this world by those most compassionate gurus. He systematically read them, stood by them and even preached them to those who were unaware of their esoteric purports. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://chameleon.tsi.lan/DevHelp/ResponsePage/5413) had no inkling or interest earlier in going to paramapdham. However, he celebrates the grace of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who had blessed him with the desire to go to paramapdham, the divine place of [sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), HIS consorts and HIS innumerable devotees.

**Explanation:**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://chameleon.tsi.lan/DevHelp/ResponsePage/5413) says “In my earlier days, I read a lot of books that were authored by our great [pUrvAchAryas](http://acharyas.koyil.org/) with the sole purpose of lifting the downtrodden chEthanas (those that has conscience) in this world. Though those books might have been authored by different [AchAryas](http://acharyas.koyil.org/), all of them resonated the same thought as though it was spoken with one neck. These books were given by the [AchAryas](http://acharyas.koyil.org/) with so much compassion towards the chEthanas. I studied whatever books I could catch hold of with interest during that time. As they say “*theriththu ezhudhi* ([nAnmugan thiruvandhAdhi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) 63)”, I even learned them methodically from my gurus. Not just learning them, I even stood by what was mentioned in those books. This extended to me preaching those who had no idea of these books. I taught them the purport of these books so that they could as well learn that which will only be beneficial for the betterment of their souls. This was how I used to spend my time in those days. I never had any inclination to go to paramapadham, the place where Lord [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) resides. I was enjoying the benefits of this world and paid no heed to go to the place where the consort of the divine [periya pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/), that is, [sriman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) (as described as “*thAmaraiyAL kELvan*” in [mudhal thiruvandhAdhi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/poigai-azhwar/) 67) lives. I never had any dream to go to that glorious place known as “paramapadham”.

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://chameleon.tsi.lan/DevHelp/ResponsePage/5413) continues, “It was not until [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) showered me with his choicest blessings that kindled the interest to go to paramapadham. His blessings are definitely something that are being celebrated by people in all eight directions. How lucky am I to get his blessings. My mind does not think about anything other thangoing to paramapadham. This is possible due to nothing but the blessings of our one and only [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).” This stress on [emperumAnAr’s](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) blessing as seen in the suffix “lE” in “aruLAlE” is of “thERRathu EkAram”.

**Footnote:** In the word “*aruLAlE*”, the author, piLLailOkam jIyar mentions about “*thERRaththu EkAram*”. It is thamizh grammar and needs a little bit of explanation. There are two types of“*EkAram*”in thamizh grammar. The first one is“*thERRaththu EkAram*”.This signifies“*urudhi*”or “certainty” or“unanimousness”.Example – In [thiruppAvai 1st pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/12/thiruppavai-01-margazhi-thingal/) where [AndAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/andal/) nails it beautifully.In“*nArAyaNanE*”, [AndAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/andal/) uses“EkAram”to mean that only[nArAyaNaN](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)can give paRai (benefit) and no body else. This is used to mean certainty about who can give mOksham and thefact that no one else can give it. This is “*thERRaththu EkAram*”.The second type is“*pirinilai EkAram*”.This means something like“even that”.That is in this example“*namakkE*”,[A](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/andal/)ndAL uses to mean that[nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) will give paRai to people like even us. Who are we? We are the ordinary (alpa) humans who go after food and other worldly pleasures thinking that is the highest form of pleasure. We are the dumbest and stupidest people and to even people like us (*namakkE*),[nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) will give. Thisconnotation is known as“*piri nilai EkAram*”. In the phrase“*eNNAdhE*”,the“*thERRathu EkAram*”is being used.


## Arththi prabandham – २९
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/10/arththi-prabandham-28/)

[![bhagavad_ramanuja_2011_may-624x907](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/bhagavad_ramanuja_2011_may-624x907.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/bhagavad_ramanuja_2011_may-624x907.jpg)

#### Introduction

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) in this pAsuram praises about the victories of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), the person who is solely responsible for destroying all hurdles that come in the way of paramapadham for [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)describes how [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)defeats his opponents, the ones who quote outside the vEdhas or distort what is being said in the vEdhas. He uses books that includes the likes of SrIbhAshyam in order to defeat them. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)praises [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s victories and subsequently sings mangaLams to them.

**pAsuram 29**

*chAruvAga madhanIRu seydhu samaNach chedikkanal koLuththiyE*  
*sAkkiyakkadalai vaRRaviththu migusAnkiya kiri muRiththida*  
*mARu seydhidu kaNAdha vAdhiyagaL vAy thagarththu aRamiguththu mEl*  
*vandha pAsupadhar sindhiyOdum vagai vAdhu seydha ethirAsanAr*  
*kURum mAkuru madhaththOdu kumArilan madham avaRRin mEl*  
*kodiya tharkka charam vittapin kuRugiya mAyAvAdhiyarai venRida*  
*mIRi vAdhil varu pArkkaran madhavilakkadik kodiyerindhu pOy*  
*mikka yAdhava madhaththai mAyththa peruvIrar nALum miga vAzhiyE!!!*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-29)

#### Word-by-Word Meanings

*chAruvAga madhanIRu seydhu* – ([SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) burnt into ashes the philosophy called “chAruvAka matham” that is defined by “prathyakshamEkam chArvAka:”, i.e., people who follow the philosophy of chAruvAka accept only those things that they see.  
*samaNach chedik kanal koLuththiyE* – ([SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/))burnt the philosophies of a weed called “samaNam” (jaina)  
*sAkkiyak kadalai vaRRaviththu* – ([SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) completely burnt and emptied the ocean known as “sAkkiyam” (baudhdha) using his works as rays of destruction  
*migusAngkiya kirimurithida –* ([SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) destroyed the philosophy called “sAnkhyam” that was largely prevalent (Because of the enormous presence, the philosophy is described as a mountain)  
thagarththu – ([SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) destroyed, using his arguments  
*vAy* – the arguments put forth  
*mARu seydhidu kaNAdha vAdhiyargaL* – as “counter arguments” by a group known as “kANAdha vAdhigaL”.  
*aRamiguththu mEl vandha* – that which kept on pounding one after another  
*pAsupadhar sindhiyOdum vagai* – like how rudhran along with his entire family ran helter skelter to save his life, even rudhran’s devotees who are called “sivasamayigaL” were made to run helter skelter by  
*vAdhu seydha ethirAsanAr* – ethirAsan using his arguments  
kodiya tharkka charam vittapin avaRRin mEl – ([SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) attacked with his arrows known as “tharka” (the art of arguing using techniques such as logic etc., ) and specifically destroyed the  
*kURum* – blabbering arguments of  
*mA* – the mighty (in terms of numer of people)  
*kuru madhaththOdu –* philosophy called “prabhAkara madham”  
*kumArilan madham* – and the philosophy called “bhAtta madham”.  
*kuRugiya mAyAvAdhiyarai venRida* – ([SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) went to the place where the people of “mAyAvAdha” philosophy lived and won over the arguments of all the people whom he was able to meet.  
*pArkkaran madha vilakkadi kodiyerindhu pOy* – ([SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) shook and plucked the fundamental arguments of people of “bhAskara” philosophy and threw them astray and went ahead.  
*mIRi vAdhil varum* – these “bhAskara” philosophy people were the people who came with so much haughtiness to argue against [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).  
*mikka yAdhava madhaththai mAyththa* – (After conquering the bhAskra philosophy, [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) totally annihilated the philosophy of “yAdhavaprakAsa”, whose followers were huge in number.  
nALum migavAzhiyE!!! – Long live  
*peruvIrar* – emperumAnAr , who has an unmatched bravery and victories over his opponents.  
****

#### Simple Translation

In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)celebrates the victories of SrI rAmAnuja. Specifically, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)lists some of the philosophies that were prevalent and famous. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)praises [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)who emerged victorious over the philosophies that includes the likes of “chAruvAka”, “samaNam”, “sAkhyam”, “sAnkhyam”, “kANAvAdhi”, ”pAsupatha”, “prabhAkara”, “bhAtta”, “mAyAvAdha” and “yAdhava”. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)concludes by saying that the victories of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)should grow daily. He sings mangaLam to such [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).

#### Explanation

The philosophy that is known as “chAruvAka matham”, whose basic tenet is “prathyakshamEva chArvAka:” (A chArvAka person accepts only what is seen by naked eye), was burnt down to ashes by the scorching rays of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)‘s arguments. He set fire to the philosophy known as “samaNam” (jainisim). The ocean called “sAkhya madham” was made completely dry without any trace of water in it by [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), again using his scorching rays of arguments. One of the philosphies that was spread in large numbers was known by the name of “sAnkhya madham”. Hence it is compared to a mighty mountain. Yet [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), using his vajrAyudham called “arguments”, annihilated this very mountain. There were some group of people known as “kANAdh vAdhigaL” who are known for their counter arguments. Sri rAmAmuja decimated their counter arguments using his arguments.

There were another group of people who were known by the name of “pAsupathars”. A lot of people belonging to this group flocked in large numbers to argue and win against [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). However, they were made to run helter skelter in order to save their livelihood by the arguments of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). This was akin to how rudhran and his entire family were made to run helter skelter by krishNa during the battle of bhANAsura. [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)wielded the powerful bow of arrows towards the arguments of people in “prabhAkara philosophy” and “bhAtta philosophy”. After doing this, he went towards the places where the people pursuing “mAyAvAdha philosophy” lived. Their presence was widely prevalent. [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)defeated them using his arguments, as celebrated by the phrase “vAdhil venRAn nammirAmAnusan ([irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) 58)”. People from “bhAskara philosophy” came to argue against [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).However, [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)not only defeated them but also ensured that no one ever walks in the path that were laid by them. There were a huge crowd from the followers of “yAdhava philosophy” that flocked together with the sole objective of defeating [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). To their utter dismay, [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)obliterated them completely without any trace of their philosophy.

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) wishes that these brave, victorious acts of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), that were the result of him destroying other philosophies, should go day by day.


## Arththi prabandham – ३०
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/10/arththi-prabandham-29/)

[![ramanujar-srirangam-2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/11/ramanujar-srirangam-2.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/11/ramanujar-srirangam-2.jpg)

#### **Introduction**

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) sings glories and mangaLams to [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) in this pAsuram starting from the latter’s lotus feet and proceeding gradually up towards his head. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)feels that [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)would have been tired after the long list of debates he had with people from other philosophies. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)envisions [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)as one who is seated with SrI bhAshyam and [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) in his hands. This striking pose captures the imagination of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)and hence he goes ahead and sings glories to each and every part of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) and wishes that each one of them should live forever.

#### **pAsuram 30**

*sIrArum ethirAsar thiruvadigaL vAzhi*  
*thiruvaraiyil sARRiya senthuvarAdai vAzhi*  
*ErArum seyyavadivu eppozhudhum vAzhi*  
*ilangiya munnUl vAzhi iNaiththOLgaL vAzhi*  
*sOrAdha thuyya seyya mugachchOdhi vAzhi*  
*thUmuRuval vAzhi thuNaimalarkkaNgaL vAzhi*  
*IrARu thirunAmam aNindha ezhil vAzhi*  
*inithiruppOdu yezhil gyAna muththirai vAzhiyE!!!*

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/arththi-prabandham-30)

#### **Word-by-Word Meanings**

vAzhi – Live for eternity!!!  
ethirAsar – [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s  
thiruvadigaL – lotus feet that is an ornament for our heads and which is an object of enjoyment  
sIr Arum – and that is replete with auspicious qualities.  
vAzhi – Live for eternity!!!  
senthuvarAdai – the saffron robe (that sanyAsis wear) that has the color of the bright sun  
sARRiya – that [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) adorns over  
thiruvaraiyil – his frame.  
vAzhi – Live for eternity!!!  
eppozhudhum – At all times  
seyyavadivu – the divine body (dhivya mangaLa vigraham) that is resplendent, shining and  
ErArum – that is filled with beauty all over it.  
vAzhi – Live for eternity!!!  
ilangiya munnUl – the sacred thread that establishes the fact that reinforces that he is the greatest student of vEdhic scriptures. The thread that is like a sheath of thunder on an evening sky known as his body, long live!!!  
vAzhi – Live for eternity!!!  
iNaiththOLgaL – the shoulders that (a) look like the branches of the golden kaRpaga tree (b) that which can grant mOksham and (c) that which possess the power to liberate a person from bondage (d) that which can uplift (a downtrodden) as well as grant (mOksham) and as a result of this characters looks hale and healthy and (e) that which adorns the beautiful, fragrant garland called “thuLasi”  
vAzhi – Live for eternity!!!  
sOrAdha thuyya cheyya mugachchOdhi – the glow of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)that does not have any bounds, is pure and effulgent. This is caused by (a) the happiness derived from seeing [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and HIS devotees (b) the process of destroying the arguments of non devotees.  
vAzhi – Live for eternity!!!  
thUmuRuval – the slight, pure, bright and beautiful smile on the face that is akin to the blossom of a flower. The smile stems from (a) protecting the refugees and (b) the enjoyment associated with emperumAn  
vAzhi – Live for eternity!!!  
thuNaimalarkkaNgaL – the pair of beautiful eyes that sees (a) SrIrangaSrI ([periya perumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)), (b) SrIvaishNavaSrI that was corrected by SrI rAmAnuja (this includes everything in this world that surrendered unto the louts feet of SrI rAmAnuja). Those eyes look with utmost compassion towards those who surrender to him and that diving glances make them pure.  
vAzhi – Live for eternity!!!  
IrAru thirunAmam aNindha ezhil – the twelve divine resplendent “thirumaN kAppu” or “Urdhva pundRam” on the glittery rose body. This is similar to seeing white lotus (thirumaN kAppu) blossoming on a golden mountain (body of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)). This thirumaN kAppu is a manifestation of the aforementioned qualities and trait of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) and is something that ensures that the “SrIvaishNavaSrI” spreads across.  
vAzhi – Live for eternity!!!  
gyAna muthirai – the pose of which [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) in which he is seen giving advice about “para thathvam”  
inithiruppOdu – having sitting in a padhmAsana posture  
yezhil – that is beautiful (because the pose represents the essence of meaning of both samskrutha and thamizh vEdhas).

#### **Simple Translation**

In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)sings maNgaLAsAsanam to [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). He starts with the divine lotus feet, the saffron robe, his whole body as such, his brahma sUthram, his powerful shoulders, his beautiful smile, his compassionate eyes, his “thirumaN kAppu” and finally the gyAna mudhrai in which he is seated among his devotees.

#### **Explanation**

In this pAsuram, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)sings glories (mangaLAsAsanam) to [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). He starts with singing glories to [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s divine lotus feet and wishes that they should live for eternity. [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is the leader of yathis and is replete with auspicious qualities pertaining to svarUpam, rUpam and characteristics, the very same qualities that are yearned by his devotees. As described as “amarar sennipU (thirukurundhAndagam 6)” and “irAmAnusan adip pU ([rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-1/)), [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s lotus feet is something that presents itself as something that is to be enjoyed fully and is something that adorns our head. Such a lotus feet should be there for eternity without anything happening to those divine lotus feet. Next, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)sings glories to the saffron robe that [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) adorns around his frame. He wishes that it should be there forever as well. \[The reason for saffron robe is explained in this section. There are two excerpts that are taken to describe the saffron color. (i) There is a chUrNikai in [SrI vachana bhUshaNam](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) that says “ARu prakAraththAlE parisudhdhAthma svarUpaththukku thathsAmyam uNdAyirukkum ([SrI vachana](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) [bhUshaNam](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) 240)”. The essence of this chUrNikai is that all souls are comparable to [periya pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/), when the souls realize their true nature. A soul has six defining characteristics that are (a) ananyArha SEshathvam or the quality of not being a servant to anyone other than [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) (b) ananya SaraNathvam or the quality of not taking refuge under anyone other than [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), (c) ananya bhOgyathvam or the quality of not being an object of enjoyment to anyone other than [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), (d) samSlEshaththil dharikkai or the quality of being able to sustain/survive \[only\] during union with[SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) (e) viSlEshaththil dhariyAmai or the quality of being unable to sustain/survive when separated from[SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and (f) thadhEka nirvAhyathvam or the quality of being controlled only by [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). When the soul is able to realize its true traits, i.e. the six aforementioned traits, due to the causeless mercy of [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), it is on par with [periya pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/) who is epitome of nAyaki lakshNam and have realized these six traits always. Now the second except is the phrase “sIthakAshAyavAsini”\]. From these excerpts, it goes to be say that the saffron is a color that signifies “pArathanthriyam” (the quality of completely dependent on the master and obeys HIM without any question) and “ananyArhathvam” (the quality by which a soul is not reserved for anyone except for [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)describes this beautiful saffron robe that is similar to sun in color and that which perfectly adorns the frame of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). Next, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)sings glories to the dhivya mangaLa vigraham (divine body) of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)describes [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s divine body as one that is extremely pleasing to those who surrender unto him. His body is full of individual features that reflects beauty at its best. The features are so soft and tender like those of a freshly blossomed flower. As they say “rUpamEvAsyai thanmahimAna mAsashtE”, [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s divine body is bright and effulgent as paramAthama ([SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)) radiates from within. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)sings glories to such a divine form that it should be there forever as per the SAsthra vAkhyam “*nithyam nithyA kruthitharam*”. Next, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)sings glories to the sacred thread (a set of three strands) that reinforce the fact that he is a great follower of vEdhic scriptures and abides by it meticulously. The sacred thread on [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s body is akin to a sheath of silver on an evening sky. Long live such a sacred thread.

Next, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)sings glories to the gorgeous shoulders of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)and wishes that they should be there forever. The greatness of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s shoulders is described in detail by [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/). As per the phrase “*bhAhuchchAyamava ashtabdhOsyapalakO mAhAthmana:*”, the shoulders of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) are something that acts like branches of the golden kaRpaga tree that provides shade, shelter and comfort to all people who are under it. The shoulders are capable of granting anyone the mOksham. They are capable of uplifting and thereby liberating the most downtrodden in this world. The shoulders are broad and big because of this ability to grant and lift people. As described in [gyAna sAram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/11/gyana-saram-english/) pAsuram “thOLAr chudarththigiri sangudaya sundharanukku ([gyAna sAram 7](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/02/gyana-saram-7-tholar-sudarth/))”, the shoulders of SrI rAmAnuja are powerful. They are adorned with garland that are made of thuLasi, vaguLam and naLinAksha flowers. [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) wishes that such matchless shoulder of SrI rAmAnuja should live forever and sings glories to them. Next, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) looks at the face of SrI rAmAnuja and starts to sing mangaLAsAsanam to it. As per the descriptive phrases like “*brahmavidha iva sowmyathE mukham pAdhi*”, and “*mugachchOdhi malarndhadhuvO* ([thiruvaimozhi 3.1.1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/thiruvaimozhi-3-1-mudichchodhi/))”, the glow of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) that does not have any bounds, is pure and effulgent. This is caused by (a) the happiness derived from seeing [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and HIS devotees (b) the process of destroying the arguments of non devotees.

Next, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) sings glories to the beautiful and charming smile of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). As per the phrase, “sa vilAsas smithAdhAram bhiprANam mukha pankajam” [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s face is compared to a beautiful lotus. In the lotus called face, there emerges a beautiful smile, as if described by AzhvAr’s “*nin pal nilA muththam thavazh kadhir muRuval* *seydhu* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 9.2.5). The cause for this smile is because of (a) happiness derived from protecting the devotees and (b) the enjoyment of being in unison with [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/).
