[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says” I do not have any lack of interest in this world, which is described as one that is cruel and to be discarded in “*koduvulagam kAttEl* ([thiruvAimozhi 4](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/11/thiruvaimozhi-4th-centum/).9.7)”. Neither do I have any interest to go to paramapdham that is described as the place that everyone should be yearning to go “*vAn ulagam theLindhE enReydhuvadhu* ([periya thirumozhi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/) 6.3.8). If this is the case, how can my father [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) happily take me to paramapadham that has no equals anywhere?


## Arththi prabandham – ४४
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/02/arththi-prabandham-43/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/antharyami.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/antharyami.jpg)

#### **Introduction**

mAmunigaL said, “*indha ulagail porundhAmai Edhumillai andha ulagil pOga Asaiyillai*” in the [previous pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/02/arththi-prabandham-43/). This means that [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says he does not have the lack of interest to continue living in this world nor does he have the desire to go to paramapadham. After saying this, he looked at other people in this world and observed their actions. He realizes the causes for these people to accrue sins incessantly. This is what is described in this pAsuram.

#### **pAsuram 44**

*mAkAntha nAraNanAr vaigum vagai aRindhOrkku*  
*EkAntham illai iruL illai*  
*mOkAnthar ivvidam yEkAntham iruL enRu bhayam aRRu irundhu*  
*seyvargaL thAm pAvaththiRam*

**Word-by-Word Meanings:**

nAraNanAr – omniscient and omnipotent [SrIman nArAyaNan,](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)  
mAkAntha – who is the consort of lakshmi  
vaigum vagai – the manner in which HE manifests Himself inside and outside of each and every sentient and non-sentient things in this universe (this meaning is impregnated in the name nArAyaNan)  
aRindhOrkku – those who know and understand it  
EkAntham illai – there is no solitude  
iruL illai – there is no darkness either.  
mOkAnthar – As described in the phrase “*mOhAntha thamasAsvruththa:*”, those people who are blinded by worldly stuff. They do not see anything and would think that  
ivvidam EkAntham iruL enRu – this place is an isolated place for there is no one  
bhayam aRRu irundhu – they will be fearless and  
seyvargaL thAm – and out of their ignorance, would continue to commit  
pAvaththiRam – more and more sins

#### **Simple Translation**

In this pAsuram, [mAmunigal](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) delineates the difference between two types of people. The first group of people see a bright [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) everywhere. Hence they never have a time when they think they are alone as they see HIS presence everywhere. They also do not see darkness as HE is full of light. On the other end of the spectrum, there is a lot of people who are not able to see this and and think that they are alone in darkness. This makes them commit innumerable sins that is the cause for their downfall.

#### **Explanation**

[nammAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) used the name “selva nAraNan” in his [thiruvAimozhi (1.10.8](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/10/thiruvaimozhi-1-10-8-selva-naranan/))”. HE is the divine consort of periyapirAtti [srImahAlakshmi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/). HE manifests inside and outside of each and every sentient and non sentient beings. This is what is conveyed as the essence of the name “nArAyaNan”. There are some people who realize this omnipresent nature of [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). These people see HIM everywhere, glowing with striking resplendence as seen in the phrases “*nArAyaNa paranjOthi:* (nArAyaNa sUktham 4)”, “*pagal kaNdEn nAraNanaikkaNdEn* [(iraNdAm thiruvandhAdhi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/bhuthaththazhwar/) 81)”, “*avan ennuL iruL thAn aRa vIRRirundhAn* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.7.3)”. They do not see solitude and darkness ever. They are never alone and are in constant company of peers. Since they are not alone, they do not have any fear whatsoever. They never see darkness anywhere as they say “*hruthi nArAyaNam paSyanApya kachchathrahasthA yassvathAradhauchApi gOvindham tham upAsmahE* (vishNu purANam)”

On the contrary, there are other group of people who are labelled as “mOhAnthakas”. As characterized by the phrase“*mOhAntha thamasA vruththA:*”, these people do not have the ability or capacity to see what lays ahead of them due to their perceived darkness. As described by “*anthar bahis sakala vasthushu santhamIsam andha: purassthithamIvahamavIkshamANa:* ([yathirAja vimshathi 12](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/08/yathiraja-vimsathi-12/))”, [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) is shining forever everywhere while manifesting equally inside and outside of every sentient and non sentient beings. People who does not see HIM with their inner eyes, they perceive something quite contrary. They see that a particular place as a place where no one is present and is a place where only darkness dwells. This triggers their fearlessness that makes them do innumerable sins as described by the phrase “*thasyAnthi kEthvam vrajinam karOshi*”. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) realizes that this is the state of these kind of people who does not see [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/).


## Arththi prabandham – ४५
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-44/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/acharya-sishya-instruction.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/acharya-sishya-instruction.jpg)

#### **Introduction**

In the previous pAsuram, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) talked about the omnipresent [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) in “*mAkAntha nAraNaNAr vaigum vagai*”. In this pAsuram he feels that he himself was the lowest of the lowest “*mOhAnthakas*” as described in the earlier pAsuram, i.e., he deems himself to be lowest person of the group of people who see only darkness and solitude for they are not able to realize [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). He feels that he failed to understand the omnipresent [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and the relationship that he shares with HIM forever. He failed to realize this and became one among the mOhAnthakas. However, in spite of all these, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) reminds to his heart, that it is purely due to the association of AchAryan, that he was uplifted for the better. This forms the crux of this pAsuram.

#### **pAsuram 45**

*nArAyaNan thirumAl nAram nAm ennum muRai*  
*ArAyil nenjE anAdhi anRO – sIrArum*  
*AchAriyanAlE anRO nAm uyndhadhu enRu*  
*kUsAmal eppozhudhum kURu*

#### **Word-by-Word Meanings**

nenjE – Oh my heart!!!  
nArAyaNan thirumAl – As described in the phrase “[*thirumAlE nAnum unakku pazhavadiyEn*](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/thiruppallandu-11-al-vazhakku/)”, Sriya:pathi [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) is the owner and master of all [souls](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/) that are collectively referred as “nAram”.  
nAram nAm – We are the souls that are eternal.  
ArAyil – If it is to be proved  
ennum muRai – that eternal relationship (between soul and SrIman nArAyaNan)  
anAdhi anRO – Is it something that started from yesterday? No. Is it not true that it is eternal (forever)? (Yes it is in fact true.)  
(hey my heart!!!)  
sIrArum – The person who showed and reinforced that relationship (to us), the very same person who is full of auspicious qualities like knowledge and the like  
AchAriyanAlE anRO – is the AchAryan. Is it not because of him, the AchAryan?  
nAm uyndhadhu enRu – The reason we got liberated is indeed because of him.  
(hey my heart)  
kURu – Please keep telling about it  
eppozhudhum – at all times  
kUsAmal – without any shame.

#### **Simple Translation**

In this pAsuram, [mAmunigal](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) talks about the greatness of AchAryan who was the person who restated and reinforced the relationship between the soul and [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). He says that the time before this reinforcement happened, he was akin to a non living thing that is not able to realize anything. Hence [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) urges his heart to state the fact that it is purely because of AchAryan’s grace that he is being uplifted and nothing else.

**Explanation:**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says “hey! my dear heart!!! [periyAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/20/periyazhwar/) had mentioned “*thirumAlE nAnum unakku pazhavadiyEn* ([thirupallAndu 11)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/thiruppallandu-11-al-vazhakku/)”. He is the Sriya:pathi, the divine consort of [SrI](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/), [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). We (souls) are known as “nAram”. The relationship between the soul and [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) is eternal and forever. If it has to be researched about the existence of this relationship, we would find that this relationship is not something that was created yesterday or some time ago. It was not created for it was always there and eternal. However, we ([mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) and his heart) did not realize this and was oblivious of this relationship and failed to take any quantum of cognizance about it. We were very much akin to non sentient being that does not have the ability to realize this relationship. But everything changed when our AchAryan made us understand this relationship and reinforced its significance. AchAryan is someone who is full of knowledge and replete with auspicious qualities. We were uplifted only because of our AchAryan. As they say “*perumaiyum nANum thavirndhu pidhaRRumin* ([thiruvAimozhi 3.5.10](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/09/thiruvaimozhi-3-5-10-karumamum/))”, please speak about this fact. Speak about it openly so that everyone knows about it”. This point is described in “*iRaiyum uyirum*” pasuram in [pramEya sAram 10](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/prameya-saram-10/).


## Arththi prabandham – ४६
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-45/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/thiruvaimozhi-pillai.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/thiruvaimozhi-pillai.jpg)

#### **Introduction**

In the previous pAsuram, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) celebrated the greatness of AchAryan by saying that it is because of his grace that he is uplifted in the first place. In this pAsuram, he describes it in more detail.

#### **pAsuram 46**

*thiruvAimozhip piLLAi thIvinaiyOndhammai*  
*guruvAgi vandhu uyyakkoNdu – poruvil*  
*madhi thAn aLiththaruLum vAzhvanRO nenjE*  
*ethirAsarkku ALAnOm yAm*

**Word-by-Word Meanings:**

nenjE – hey my heart!!!  
yAm – We  
ALAnOm – became the servants of  
ethirAsarkku – for [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)

(The reason for it is because)  
[thiruvAimozhip piLLAi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) – thiruvAimozhip piLLAi (the AchAryan of [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/))  
guruvAgi – incarnated as AchAryan  
vandhu – and came to the place where we were.  
thIvinayOndhammmai – We, who are verily the clouds of cruel sins  
uyyakkoNdu – were approved by his grace and were deemed “upliftable”.  
aLiththaruLum – He also blessed us by giving  
madhi thAn – the knowledge that evolves from knowing [thirumanthram](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2015/12/rahasya-thrayam.html)  
poruvil – that is incomparable (unlike the likes of SAsthrams and their subsequent knowledge that might have comparables)  
vAzhvanRO – (hey my heart!!!) Is it not because of this great opportune? (it is indeed because of him that we became the servants of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)

#### **Simple Translation**

In this pAsuram, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) celebrates the greatness of his AchAryan. He says that it is because he came to the place where he was and gave [thirumanthram](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2015/12/rahasya-thrayam.html), he was able to be a servant of the servant of the Lord [srIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/).

#### **Explanation**

The greatness of [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) is described first. “thiruvAimozhi” is a divine prabandham that is a nector to all devotees of [SrIman nArAyanAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) (who are SrIvaishNavas who are also known as bhUsurar (the celestial beings of this world)) as [nammAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) himself said “*thoNdarkkamudhuNNach chol mAlaigaL sonnEn* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 9.4.9). [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) is an AchAryan who used to breathe [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) and live in it. He enjoyed the different types of nectarines in it namely nectarine that comes from the arrangement of words, nectarine that comes from the meanings and the nectarine that oozes from sheer passion involved in the pAsurams. He lived by the purport of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) and considered all other SAsthrams to be like grass. He performed all types of kainkaryam to nammAzhvAr at all times by surrendering to his lotus feet. Since he was known to the world by his association with [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), he became to be known as “[thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)”. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says to his heart “hey my dear heart! Look at us. We verily represent the cloud of cruel sins as described in the phrase “*oppillAth thIvinaiyEnai uyyakkoNdu* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 7.9.4)”. [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)incarnated as AchAryan and liberated us”. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) himself quotes this in his upadhESa raththina mAlai pAsuram as per “*thEnAr kamalath thirumAmagaL kozhunan thAnE guruvAgi* ([upadEsa raththina mAlai 61](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/02/upadhesa-raththina-malai-61/))”. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) continues, “He came to the place where we were and gave us the knowledge that has its genesis from [thirumanthram](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2015/12/rahasya-thrayam.html). This is different from the knowledge that stems from other SAsthrams. Hey my heart! Is it not because of this great opportunity that we were uplifted and got the golden opportunity of serving our master [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)? In fact it is and it is the only reason why we even got this opportunity in the first place. The highest meaning that is conveyed in [thirumanthram](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2015/12/rahasya-thrayam.html) is being servant to the servants of the Lord [SrIman nArAyanAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/). It is because of realization of this fact, that we in fact became eternal servants of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)”.


## Arththi prabandham – ४७
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-46/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/emperumanar-vanamamalai.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/emperumanar-vanamamalai.jpg)

#### **Introduction**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) being pleased saying “*ethirAsarkkALAnOm yAm*“, desiring to reveal the greatness of the divine name “[*rAmAnuja*](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/emperumanar/)” which is different from and more ingenious than the divine name “[*nArAyaNa*](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)” which was previously spoken about in “*mAkAntha nAraNanAr*” and “*nArAyaNan thirumAl*“, does so in vyathirEka (negation).

#### **pAsuram 47**

*irAmAnusAya namavenRu iravum pagalum sindhiththirA*  
*mAnusargaL iruppidam thannil iRaippozhudhumirA*  
*mAnusar avarkku ellA adimaiyum seyyaveNNi*  
*irA mAnusar thammai mAnusarAga enkol eNNuvadhE*

#### **Word-by-Word Meanings**

mAnusargaL – (There are) some people  
irA – who do not  
iravum pagalum – day and night  
sindhiththu – meditate upon  
irAmAnusAya – [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)  
namavenRu – by uttering “irAmAnusAya nama:” (translated loosely to “I am not for myself, I am for [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)”)  
mAnusar avarkku – there are some people (like [kUraththAzhvAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/kUraththAzhwAn/))  
irA – who do not live  
iRaippozhudhum – even for a small fraction of a second  
iruppidam thannil – in the aforementioned group of people’s place (who does not say “irAmAnusAya nama:” day in and day out)  
mAnusar thammai – people  
irA – who does not  
seyyaveNNi – perform  
ellA adimaiyum – all kinds of kainkaryam (to people like [kUraththAzhvAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/kUraththAzhwAn/)),  
mAnusarAga enkol eNNuvadhE – how can they be considered as humans, they are similar to mere cows.

#### **Simple Translation**

There are three groups of people. For the sake of simplicity, lets us call them Group A, Group B and Group C. Group A are those people who does not say “irAmAnusAya nama:” day and night. People in Group B would never live in the company of Group A people. An example of Group B people is [kUraththAzvAn](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/10/05/kurathazhwan/). The last group of people, people in Group C are those who fail to recognize the greatness of people in Group B and so would never want to do incessant kainkaryam to them. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) questions as to how can he consider people in Group C as humans, when in fact they are mere animals, such as a cow for their acts.

#### **Explanation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says “Each and everyone should mediate upon the sacred manthra of “*irAmAnusAya nama:*” incessantly. They should do this without differentiating between day and night, as described by the [thirumangai AzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/) in “*naLLiruL aLavum pagalum nAn azhaippan* (periya thirumozhi 1.1.15)”. Yet, there are lots of people who does not do this. One should realize that he or she should not be in the company of such people who does not meditate upon the sacred manthrA of “*irAmAnusAya nama:*”. He or she should never have any sort of attachment or affection with these people who are comparable to a cow. He or she (as the likes of [kUraththAzhvAn](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/10/05/kurathazhwan/) et al), who lives by the SAsthra, should never be in touch with these kind of people. Secondly, it is important to know, understand and appreciate the greatness of this group of people who has no connection with the earlier group who does not meditate upon the sacred manthrA of “*irAmAnusAya nama:*”. To such elevated souls, one should strive to do kainkaryam eternally as revealed by [thiruvarangathamudhAnAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/amudhanar/) in “*eththozhumbum sollAl manaththAl karumathinAl seyvan sOrvinRiyE* ([irAmnusa nURRandhAdhi 80](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/02/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-80/))”. People who does not do this kainkaryam to such elite people, are deemed to be worthy comparison to cows as pointed out by “*mAnidavarallar enrE en manaththE vaithEn*”. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) finally concludes by asking himself a questions, “How can I consider these people to be humans in the first place, if they do not do kainkaraym to the group of people who does not stay in the company of the group of people who does not meditate upon the sacred manthrA of ‘*irAmAnusAya nama*:’? I can never imagine them as humans in the first place”.


## Arththi prabandham – ४८
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-47/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/09/periyaperumal-art-4.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/09/periyaperumal-art-4.jpg)

#### **Introduction**

In the [previous pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-47/), [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) mentioned about doing all kinds of kainkaryam to devotees. While using the word “*irAmAnusAya nama:*”, he got reminded of who gave him this mind of doing kainkaryam. In this pAsuram, he explains that it was [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) who blessed his senses and organs to do kainkaryam for [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) and his devotees. He says this very gleefully.

#### **pAsuram 48**

*eNNAdhu ennenjam isaiyAdhu en nAvu irainjAdhu senni*  
*kaNNAnavai onRum kANaluRA kaliyAr naliya*  
*oNNAdha vaNNam ulagu aLiththOn ethirAsan adi*  
*naNNAdhavarai arangEsar seydha nalam namakkE!!!*

#### **Word-by-Word Meanings**

naNNAdhavarai – There are people who does not take refuge at  
ethirAsan adi – the lotus feet of [SrI emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), who  
aLiththOn – protected  
ulagu – the worldly  
kaliyAr – people of kali yugam, who have conscience  
naliya oNNAdha vaNNam – from being pounced by the cruelities of kali  
ennenjam – (Towards such people) my heart will not  
eNNAdhu – think about them.  
en nAvu – My speech  
isaiyAdhu – will not be about them , be it talk / praise.  
senni – My head  
irainjAdhu – will not bow down (towards them).  
kaNNAnavai – My eyes  
onRum kANaluRA – will not see anything (related to them).  
arangEsar – It was periya perumAL who gave me the thoughts and the senses associated with it.  
seydha nalam namakkE – these senses does not go subservient to someone else. They are deserved only for SrI rAmAnuja. This great help was possible solely by the blessings of namperumAL  
(kaliyAr naliya oNNAdha vaNNam ulagaLiththAn yathirAsAn – This phrase could also mean “[SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who protected the world from the brunt of the cruel kali).

#### **Simple Translation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says that his mind, eyes, mouth and head will never do what they are supposed to do, when it comes to facing the people who do not surrender to the lotus feet of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). He says that his eyes will not see them, his head will not bow down, his mind will not think and his mouth will not talk about them. He celebrates that this blessed opportunity was bestowed upon him by the infinite mercy of [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) SrIrangarAjan.

#### **Explanation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says “[emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) protected this world from the wrath of the cruel kali as mentioned in “*thAzhvonRillA maRai thAzhndhu thala muzhudhum kaliyE ALginRa nALvandhAliththavan* ([irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi 16](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-16/))”. As described in the phrase “*pEr onRu maRRillai* ([irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi 45](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/08/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-45/))”, the means and the final destination are
[emperumAnAr’s](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) lotus feet. Those who do not realize this and surrender unto the lotus feet of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), this is how my senses and organs will behave. My mind and heart goes out, celebrates and immerses itself in the glorious attributes of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) as described by “*naiyum manam un guNangaLai eNNi*” and ““*nithyam yathIndhra* ([yathirAja vimSathi 4](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/08/yathiraja-vimsathi-4/))”. But when it comes to those people who do not surrender unto the lotus feet of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), all my senses including my heart will stop thinking, praising, talking and seeing. The reason for this particular behavior of mine is due to [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) SrI rangarAjan’s infinite mercy. “nalam” that is used in conjunction with “*naNNAdhavarai arangEsar seydha nalam*” means “wealth” here. As per the phrase “*mana:pUrvO vAguththara:*”, the speech/mouth is closely associated with the mind as it acts as a channel to let the thoughts that emanate from the mind in the first place. However, my mouth will not talk about them nor praise them as in “*nAviyal isai mAlaigaL yEththi* ([thiruvAimozhi 4.5.4](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/02/thiruvaimozhi-4-5-4-mevi-ninru/))”. My head that goes and bows down to SrI rAmAnuja as in “*praNamAmi mUrdhnA* ([thaniyan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thaniyans-invocation/) by [kUraththAzhvAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/kUraththAzhwAn/))” would never bow to those people. As described by “*kaN karudhidum kANa* ([irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) 102)” and “*SrI mAdhavAngri* ([yathirAja vimSathi 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/08/yathiraja-vimsathi-1/)”, my eyes will never see them. The word “*kaliyAr*” is personification of kali yuga. It goes to prove that the evil and cruel effects of kali are so powerful that one gets fear instilled and call them with respect out of fear for it as seen in the usage “*EvinAr kaliyAr* ([periya thirmozhi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/) 1.6.8”)


## Arththi prabandham – ४९
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-48/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/thiruvarangathu-amudhanar.emperumAnAr-at-heart.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/08/thiruvarangathu-amudhanar.emperumAnAr-at-heart.jpg)

**Introduction**

In the earlier pAsuram, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) revealed his lack of interest towards mundane people of this earth by saying “*ethirAsan adi naNNAdhavarai eNNAdhu*”. However, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) who is characterized by a soft, gentle and warming heart towards everyone, could not bear the abysmal state in which his fellow people (earthlings) were. Out of sheer compassion towards fellow human beings, he shows them the path to salvation in [emperumAnAr’s](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) lotus feet and lays the rules for it.

**pAsuram 49**

*nandhA naragaththu azhundhAmai vENdidil nAnilaththIr*  
*en thAdhaiyAna ethirAsanai naNNum enRum avan*  
*andhAdhi thannai anusandhiyum avan thoNdarudan*  
*sindhAkulam kedach chErndhirum muththi pin siththikumE!!!*

**Word-by-Word Meanings:**

nAnilaththIr – Hey!!! People of this world that are of four types!!!  
vENdidil – if you wish to  
azhundhAmai – not be imbibed in  
naragaththu – the hell that is also known as “samsAra sAgaram” or “worldly hell”  
nandhA – which cannot be completed anytime by experiencing  
(then listen to me)  
naNNum – go and take refuge at  
en – my  
thAdhaiyAna – father  
ethirAsanai – emperumAnAr.  
anusandhiyum – chant and medidate  
enRum – at all times  
avan andhAdhi thannai – [irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/), that serves as “*prapanna gAyathri*” and that which resonates the name of emperumAnAr that paves way for salvation.  
chErndhirum – be at the service of  
avan thoNdarudan – his devotees who are the finest srivaishNavAs.  
sindhAkulam – the pain and pangs caused by association with other things in this world  
keda – will be obliterated upon which  
muththi – salvation  
pin siththikumE – will ensue at the opportune moment

**Simple Translation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/), in this pAsuram, looks at the pitiable state of worldly people and tells them of an easy route to get liberated. He urges those who wish to be liberated from shackles of this world that is also regarded as hell, to go unto the lotus feet of his father [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). He asks them to chant and meditate “[irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/)” that has the names of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) in every one of the verses. He asks them to be at the service of the devotees of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). This would obliterate all sorts of pains and sufferings one would have experienced before taking shelter at the lotus feet of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) assures that when the opportune time presents itself, they will be liberated for sure.

**Explanation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says “This world is verily described as hell in our scriptures. To quote a few from [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)‘ pAsurams, “*nandhA naragaththazhundhA vagai* ([periya thirumozhi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/) 11.8.9)”, “*naragaththidai naNungA vagai* ([periya thirumozhi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/) 7.9.5)” and “*maRRai naragam* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.1.9)”. The experience, pains and sufferings in this hell known as “world”, is something that does not have an end at any point in time. It just goes on and on. Hey! my dear fellow earthlings who live in this world that are of four types!!! If you want to escape from this hell and not be immersed and imbibed in this hell and want to be liberated from its wrath, here is what you should do. Please go towards my father [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) and take refuge under him. His very names that pave way for salvation are in each and every poem of “[irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/)” that is also known as “prapanna gAyathri” \[that which is to be recited by prapannas every day, without fail\]. Go ahead and meditate upon those names. As described in [irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/), “*un thoNdargaLukkE* – ([irAmAnusa nURRandhAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) 107)”, please go and always strive at the lotus feet of the devotees of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). All your sufferings associated with whatever association you had hitherto will be obliterated without any trace. Upon this, you will be liberated at the opportune moment.


## Arththi prabandham – ५०
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-49/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/paramapadham.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/paramapadham.jpg)

#### **Introduction**

People who were referred in the earlier pAsuram, were ready to take refuge under the lotus feet of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) gives them another piece of critical advice wondering why are they wasting their time doing insignificant, inconsequential and trivial things. He says that upon chanting the names of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), they are destined to get the most coveted prize that anyone could ask for.

#### **pAsuram 50**

*avaththE arumandha kAlaththaip pOkki aRivinmaiyAl*  
*pavaththE uzhalginRa pAviyargAL palakAlam ninRu*  
*thavaththE muyalbavar thangatkum eydhavoNNAdha*  
*andhath thivaththE umai vaikkum sindhiyum nIr ethirAsarenRu*

**Word-by-Word Meanings:**

pAviyargAL – Hey!!! sinners!  
aRivinmayAl – Out of sheer ignorance  
uzhalginRa – (you people are) dwelling  
pavaththE – in this mundane world and  
avaththE pOkki – wasting (just like that)  
arumandha kAlaththai – the precious time when the names of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) could have been chanted and meditated easily  
andhaththivaththE – [paramapadham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/tag/paramapadham/) that is being described by the Sruthis as “parama vyOma:”  
eydhavoNNAdha – is a place that cannot be achieved by even  
muyalbhavar thangatkum – those who try their hands hard at it  
thavaththE – by means of thapas (penance).  
nIr – you people  
palakAlam – at all times  
ninRu – with undivided attention  
ethirAsarenRu sindhiyum – think about him ([SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) or yathirAja) in your heart (the effort is super small yet the result is humongous).  
umai – If you people (nithya samsAris) do it, then  
vaikkum – it will keep you people one among the elite cream of nithyasUris.

#### **Simple Translation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) talks to the worldly people, “There are many people who are striving to reach paramapadham out of their hardcore penance and steadfastness. They are unable to reach there. You people , on the contrary, have wasted all your time doing trivial, insignificant and unimportant things. Yet, there is an easy way out for you to reach [paramapadham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/tag/paramapadham/). Chant and meditate upon the names of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). It will elevate you to [paramapadham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/tag/paramapadham/) without fail.

#### **Explanation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) calls out the people in this world , “hey sinners of this world! You have wasted all the golden time earlier in life where you could have chanted the glorious names of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). Those times have gone and looking back at it, you can realize that they were wasted just like that. In spite of that, there is something so coveted and valuable waiting for you people with your smallest of your efforts. Allow me to explain. [paramapadham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/tag/paramapadham/) is a place that is celebrated in the Sruthis as “*thath aksharE paramavyOma:*” In that place, nithyasUris reside. This place is the ultimate place as the name would suggest ([paramapadham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/tag/paramapadham/)). There are many people who indulge themselves in steadfast penance striving to get to this place. Even to those people it is not something that they can get out of their volition or efforts. Yet, there is an absolute easy way to reach there. The way is nothing but chanting and meditating the glorious names of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) in your heart. This will automatically take you there. The effort is very trivial yet the result or prize for that is the ultimate that is nothing but [paramapadham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/tag/paramapadham/).


## Arththi prabandham – ५१
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-50/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/emperumAnAr_mElkote.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/emperumAnAr_mElkote.jpg)

#### Introduction

As emperumAnAr ponders “Why should you speak about other mundane persons? What was your state previously?”, mAmunigaL says “I too was like them, wasting my time since time immemorial, and was not feeling sorry for what I was missing. For such me, by the grace of your highness, I have now realized the sorrow of what I was missing for so long” and speaks about his own benefit.

#### **pAsuram 51**

*enRuLan Isan uyirum anRE uNdu ikkAlam ellAm  
inRaLavAgap pazhudhE kazhindha iruvinaiyAl*  
*enRu izhavinRi irukkum ennenjam iravu pagal*  
*ninRu thavikkum ethirAsA nI aruL seydha pinnE!!!*

#### **Word-by-Word Meanings:**

enRuLan Isan – As per the phrase, “*nAn unnai anRi ilEn kaNdAy nAraNanE ni ennai anRi ilai*” (nAnmugan thiruvandhAdhi 7), the relationship between the [paramathmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and the souls ([jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)) is eternal and cannot be broken by anyone at any point of time. This would mean that the supreme controller ISwaran [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) is there forever. On the same token,  
uyirum – the soul that is being controlled by the controller [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)  
anRE uNdu – also is forever.  
ikkAlam ellAm – For all these time,  
inRaLavAga – till now,  
iruvinaiyAl – because of my powerful karma (that includes both good and bad)  
pazhudhE kazhindha enRu – I had spent these times as “utterly wasted”.  
izhavinRi irukkum – Even worse, I have not even repented for this loss of mine.  
ethirAsA – (However) [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)!!!  
nI aruL seydha pinnE – After you showerd your choicest blessings on me!!!  
ennenjam – my heart  
ninRu – steadfastedly  
thavikkum – started to repent for it  
iravu pagal – day and night.

#### **Simple Translation**

In this pAsuram, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) celebrates the blessings of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) on him that made him to repent for the wasted time till now. Before [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) blessed [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/), the latter did not even repent for the time he lost that includes time from immemorial till now. But all that changed as [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) blessed [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) and the latter is thinking day and night only about it.

**Explanation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says “As per the words of [thirumazhisai AzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumazhisai-azhwar/), “*nAn unnai anRi ilEn kaNdAy nAraNanE ni ennai anRi ilai*” (nAnmugan thiruvandhAdhi 7), the relationship between the paramathmA [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and the souls (jIvAthmA) is eternal and cannot be broken by anyone at any point of time. This would mean that the supreme controller ISwaran [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) is there forever. On the same token, the one who is being controlled, that are known as “soul” or “jIvAthmA” is also forever. These mean that there was not a point in time when they were created. The supreme lord [SrIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and all the souls were there forever. However, till this point now when you ([emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) showered your choicest blessings on me due toyour infinite compassion, I have spent all the time by reaping the effects of my powerful karma (both good and bad). Even worse than that is, I have never repented for the time that was utterly wasted. But after your blessings fell on me, I have been only thinking about my loss and repenting day and night about it. What infinite mercy and what compassion towards me!!!


## Arththi prabandham – ५२
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-51/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/namperumal-garudan-2.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/namperumal-garudan-2.jpg)

#### **Introduction**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) said that he had the opportunity to repent for his wasted/lost time hitherto. This was possible only due to the blessings showered on him by [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) out of his infinite mercy. Subsequently, in this pAsuram, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) celebrates the manner in which [periya perumaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) would come unto him, for [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s sake. He describes how he would come to him as revealed in the phrase “*SrImAn samArUdapadhangarAja:*”.

#### **pAsuram 52**

*kanaka giri mEl kariya mugil pOl*  
*vinadhai siRuvan mERkoNdu*  
*thanuvidum pOdhu ErAr arangar ethirAsarkkAga enpAl*  
*vArA munniRppar magzhindhu*

#### **Word-by-Word Meanings**

kariya mugil pOl – Just like the clouds that hover over the  
kanaka giri mEl – top of a golden mountain called “mEru”,  
arangar – periya perumAL  
siRuvan – will come on top of the one who is known as “vainathEyan” and “periya thiruvadi” and is the son of  
vinadhai – a lady called “vinathA”.  
mERkoNdu – periya perumAL will come riding on top of vinadhai siRuvan as the latter is HIS transport.  
thanuvidum pOdhu – When my body would eventually fall  
arangar – periya perumAL who is  
Ar – replete with  
Er – beauty etc  
enpAl vArA – will came to the place where I will be  
ethirAsarkkAga – for the sake of [yathirAja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).  
(Just like how a mother shows up)  
munniRppar – HE will stand in front of me  
magizhndhu – with much happiness  
([periya perumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) will show up and show his face and smile and will enjoy me. This is certain).

#### **Simple Translation**

In this pAsuram, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) celebrates the manner in which [periya perumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) will come during his last moments. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says that HE will come on top of his transport, also known as “vinadhai siRuvan”, “periya thiruvadi” etc. HE will come to the place where I will be and show HIS beautiful smiling face. HE will do all these for the sake of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).

#### **Explanation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says, “As per the phrases in ‘*kAnchanaspa girES SrunghE sagatiththO yadhOyadhA*‘ and “*manjuyar ponmalai mEl ezhundha mAmugil pOnRuLar* ([periya thirumozhi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/) 9.2.8)”, there are black hued rain bearing clouds that hover over the great golden mountain of “*mEru*”. Similarly, when I leave my mortal coils in this earth, [periya perumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) will come atop garudan as described in “*perum pavvam maNdiyuNda peru vayiRRa karu mugil* ([thirunedunthAndakam](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/) 24). garudan is also known as “periya thiruvadi” or “vinadhai siRuvan” for he is the son of “vinathA”. At the time of me leaving this body, [periya perumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) will come, similar to how a mother would come. HE who is replete with all genres of beauty, will come to the place where I will be at that time. HE will come gleefully for [emperumAnAr’s](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) sake. HE will show his smiling face to me. This is certain.


## Arththi Prabandham – ५३
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-52/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/periyaperumAL-udayavar.png)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/periyaperumAL-udayavar.png)

#### **Introduction**

In the previous pAsuram, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) described how [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) would come unto him during his final moments of leaving his mortal coil in this world. He said that [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) would in fact come on HIS transport viz periya thiruvadi. This raises the questions “OK. What will [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) do in the mean time until his final moments come where [periya perumaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) would be present?”. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says “for that ultimate moment to happen, this body of mine, that is the source of all sins and subsequent sufferings in this world, has to fall. I cannot forever be suffering the pains caused by the sins which is in turn triggered by the very existence of this physical body. So, hey [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)!!!, You give me what is needed and best. You should liberate me from this world that is so filled with troubles and pain”.

#### **pAsuram 53**

*idhaththAlE thennarangar seygiRadhu enRaRindhE*  
*irundhAlum thaRkAla vEdhanaiyin kanaththAl*  
*padhaiththu AvO ennum indhap pAva udambudanE*  
*pala nOvum anubaviththu ippavaththu irukkappOmO?*  
*madhaththAlE valvinaiyin vazhi uzhanRu thirindha*  
*valvinaiyEn thannai unakku ALAkkik koNda*  
*idhath thAyum thandhaiyumAm ethirAsA! Ennai*  
*inik kaduga ippavaththininRum eduththaruLE!!!*

#### **Word-by-Word Meanings**

idhaththAlE – Because of “hitham” (quality of always thinking and doing that which is good towards a person)  
thennarangar – periya perumAL (SrI ranganAthan)  
seygiRadhu enRaRindhE irundhAlum – out of his mercy, is letting me suffer the wrath of my karma. Though I know that HE is doing this for my good,  
thaRkAla vEdhanaiyin kanaththAl – the sufferings that I had to undergo at that point in time (momentary pain), makes me  
padhaiththu – writhed with pain and  
AvO ennum – utter exclamations like “hA”, “Oh” that are clearly representative sounds of sufferings and pain.  
irukkappOmO? – will I be able to live  
ippavaththu – in this samsAram (mundane world)?  
indhap pAva udambudanE – with this body that is a sin by itself  
pala nOvum anubaviththu – and continue to suffer a multitude of sufferings?  
madhaththAlE – Due to the association with this body  
valvinaiyin vazhi uzhanRu thirindha – (I have) wandered in the path set by my karmAs and continued that endless journey.  
valvinaiyEn thannai – Me, the most cruel sinner of all  
ALAkkik koNda – was made your servant by you ([emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/))  
unakku – who is the base for all souls.  
idhath thAyum – (You did this as) my mother who does “hitham” and also as my  
thandhaiyumAm – father.  
ethirAsA! – hey! [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)!!!  
ini – here after  
kaduga – quickly  
eduththaruLE – uplift and liberate  
ennai – me  
ippavaththininRum – from this samsAram

**Simple Meanings**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) continues to plead to [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) to get him liberated. He realizes that his sufferings are because [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/), out of his good nature, wants the effects of his karma to be finished and so is letting him suffer. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says that though he is able to understand why [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) is doing that, he says at the time of suffering the wrath of karma, it is unbearable. It is because of his association with the body that he is into this endless journey filled with thorns of pain. Hence, he requests [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), who is his mother as well as the father, to get him liberated from this sinful world as quickly as possible.

**Explanation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says – As mentioned in the pAsuram “*ArapperunthuyarE seydhidinum* ([gyAna sAram 21](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/?p=1488))” and similar pAsurams, I do understand that it is because of HIS “hitham” (the quality of always thinking and doing only what is good towards a person), and his blessing that I am suffering a lot (that is because the karmas need to be gone somehow and so one has to undergo the suffering). Even though I realize this and understand it, when it comes to that time of suffering, it pains me a lot. It pains me so much that I exclaim words like “hA” and “Oh” that clearly shows how frustrating it is. I am uttering these words with this body that is the verily the source of all sins. I am suffering like this in this world for a long time. Is it appropriate for me to be like this forever? As [thirumangai AzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/) says “*pAvamE seydhu pAvi AnEn* (periya thirumozhi 1.9.9)”, I am committing nothing but sins. I am doing that because of my association with this body. I am being pulled into the path in which my body pulls, which unfortunately is filled with sins. As a result, I am reaping the effects of my incessant sins and am writhing each and every moment of this journey. However [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)!!! You my father and mother who does things for me for my overall betterment out of your “hitham” quality, you have blessed me and approved me. Hence, I request you to uplift me from my incessant sufferings and get me liberated from the shackles of this samsAram.


## Arththi prabandham – ५४
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-53/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/ramanuja-showing-paramapadham.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/ramanuja-showing-paramapadham.jpg)

#### **Introduction**

mAmunigaL continued to plead with [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) in the earlier pAsuram and request him to uplift from this world and get him liberated. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) knew that [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) would yield to his requests. However, that does not suffice for [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/). It is because, as they say “*oru pagal Ayiram UzhiyAy* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.3.1)”, each passing moment for mAmunigaL in this world feels like eons. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) requests [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), “You are my relative of all sorts. You should not let me go through this suffering with this body in this world. I do not know when will you liberate me from this place and transport me to the place where there is infinite bliss (paramapadham)”.

#### **pAsuram 54**

*innam eththanai nAL ivvudambudan*  
*irundhu nOvu padakkadavEn aiyO*  
*ennai idhininRum viduviththu nIr*  
*enRu thAn thirunAttinuL yERRuvIr*  
*annaiyum aththanum allAdha suRRamum Agi*  
*ennai aLiththaruL nAdhanE*  
*en idhaththai irAppagal inRiyE*  
*EgameNNum ethirAsa vaLLalE !!!*

#### **Word-by-Word Meanings**

nAdhanE – Hey!!! my master  
aLiththaruL – (You) bless  
ennai – me  
Agi – by being my  
annaiyum – mother who shows priyam,  
aththanum – (by being) a father who does hitham and  
allAdha suRRamum – (by being) all those desirable and closely knit relations.  
ethirAsa vaLLalE – the magnanimous leader of all yathis (ascetics), one who is known as “emperumAnAr”!!!  
irAppagal inRiyE EgameNNum – (One who) thinks day and night with undivided attention about  
en – my  
idhaththai – wish (only thost that proves good for me)  
(Even after falling at your lotus feet)  
eththanai nAL – how much  
innam – longer  
nOvu padakkadavEn – I have to suffer  
ivvudambudanE irundhu – in (with) this body?  
aiyO – alas!!!  
viduviththu – Please liberate  
ennai – me  
idhininRum – from this body that serves as the obstacle!!!  
enRu thAn – when will  
nIr – you  
ERRuvIr – carry me to  
thirunAttinuL – paramapadham?

#### **Simple Translation**

In this pAsuram, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says that [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is his mother, father and his every kindof good relative. He always thinks about the well being of [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/). Hence, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) asks him when he will be liberated from this bondage and grant him paramapadham, the place of infinite bliss? How long should he suffer with this body in this world.

#### **Explanation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says, “As [madhurakavi AzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/madhurakavi-azhwar/) said ‘*annaiyAy aththanAy ennai ANdidum thanmaiyAn* ([kaNNinun chiruth thAmbu 4](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/?p=1322))’, [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! You are my mother who showers a lot of love to her child. You are my father who wishes for all good things for his child. You are my closely knit relative who leadsa life of high valued principles. You are the leader of the yathis! As they say, “*en manamEgamennum irAppagalinRiyE* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 9.3.7)”, you think about my well being day and night with undivided attention. Even after surrendering unto your lotus feet as described in “*unakkAtppattum adiyEn innum uzhalvEnO* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 5.8.10)”, how much longer am I supposed to suffer with this mortal coil of mine in this world? Alas!!! When will you liberate me from this obstacle called “body” and liberate me to paramapadham, the place of infinite bliss? That day will be one unparalleled day. vaLLal would mean – a magnanimous person to whom one cannot reciprocate anything for the good deeds he did.


## Arththi prabandham – ५५
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-54/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/srisailesa-thanian-mamunigal-eedu-goshti.jpeg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/srisailesa-thanian-mamunigal-eedu-goshti.jpeg)

#### **Introduction**

As a true Sishya and an ardent follower, one needs to be cognizant of two things viz.,

\(a\) thinking about all the benefits one’s AchAryan has done unto him and

\(b\) interest towards any deed that the AchAryan will do to him in the future.

This pAsuram specifically talks about the former. [mAmunigAL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) celebrates the glorious qualities that [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) gave him. He lists them and eventually says that it is because of [emperumAnAr’s](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) grace that he was able to get these qualities.

#### **pAsuram 55**

*thennarangar sIr aruLukku ilakkAgap peRROm*  
*thiruvarangam thirupadhiyE iruppAgap peRROm*  
*manniya sIr mARankalai uNavAgap peRROm*  
*madhurakavi soRpadiyE nilaiyAgap peRROm*  
*munnavarAm nankuravar mozhigaLuLLap peRROm*  
*muzhudhum namakkavai pozhudhupOkkAgap peRROm*  
*pinnai onRu thanil nenju pErAmaRpeROm*  
*piRar minukkam poRAmayillAp perumaiyum peRROmE!!!*

#### **Word-by-Word Meanings**

ilakkAgap peRROm – (We) became the target of  
sIr aruLukku – causeless mercy of  
thennarangar – periya perumAL, who is reclining south facing in the direction of SrIlankA, in a place that is very pleasing to the eyes and is known by the name of “kOyil”, where HE captivated HIS devotees by blessing them (“*aruL koduthittu adiyavarai AtkkoLvAn amarum Ur* (periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 4.9.3))  
iruppAgap peRROm – (We) got the glorious opportunity of being permanent residents of  
thiruvarangam thirupadhiyE – [SrIrangam](http://acharya.org/dd/a/srirangam.html) that is described as “*thennAdum vadanAdum thozha ninRa thiruvarangam thiruppadhi* ([periyAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyazhwar/) thirumozhi 4.9.11)”, “*ArAmam sUzhndha arangam* ([siRiya thirumadal](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/) 71)”, “*thalaiyarangam* ([iraNdAm thiruvandhAdhi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/bhuthaththazhwar/) 70)”. It is the chief of all the [108 dhivyadhEsams](https://koyil.org/index.php/dhivya-dhesams/).  
uNavAgap peRROm – (We) Our food is  
kalai – the nectarine pAsurams of (nectarine for devotees that serves as garland for the Lord)  
mARan – [nammAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/)  
manniya sIr – who is full of auspicious qualities starting with parabhakti etc  
nilaiyAgap peRROm – (We) attained the last frontier of “*charama parva nishtai*”, that is celebrated as “*yathIndhramEva nIrandhram hishEvE dhaivathambaram*” etc. Myself and my associates started to talk about it “*unnayozhiya oru dheyvam maRRaRiyA mannupugazh sEr [vaduganambi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vaduga-namb) thannilaiyai* ([Arththi prabandham 11](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-11/))”).  
soRpadiyE – (This tenet of charama parva nishtai (regarding one’s AchAryan as everything) is derived from the) divine words of  
madhurakavi – [madhurakavi AzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/madhurakavi-azhwar/) who said “*thEvu maRRaRiyEn* ([kaNNinun chiRuth thAmbu 2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/?p=1309))”. (We got to live and abide by the tenets of the great [madhurakavi AzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/madhurakavi-azhwar/)).  
munnavarAm nankuravar mozhigaLuLLap peRROm – We got to live, breathe and explore our ancestors’ works, their divine and esoteric purports. These are the works of AchAryas who lived by the way shown by [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/).  
muzhudhum namakkavai pozhudhupOkkAgap peRROm – (We) spent our times dwelling on that (works). Our minds does not go to anything that is not these divine works of our ancestors.  
pinnai nenju pErAmaRpeROm – Our hearts and minds were so grounded to these works our ancestors that it never went behind  
onRu thanil – any of the other works apart from our ancestors’ works.  
piRar minukkam poRAmaiyillA – If the aforementioned qualities of ours that we got by the grace of emperumAnAr is placed on one side of a balance, then this one that am going to say would equal or weigh more than all of the above together. If such a rare SrIvaishnava is found with all of the aforementioned qualities, as described by “*ippadi irukkum SrIvaishNavargaL ERRam aRindhu ugandhu irukkaiyum* ([mumukshupadi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) dhvaya prakaNam 116)”, then we never become jealous seeing them. Such is our glory that was bestowed upon us by [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).  
perumaiyum peRROmE – We got this! Alas! What a great fortune to have gotten this , thanks to [emperumAnAr’s](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) causeless mercy.

#### **Simple Translation**

In this pAsuram, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) celebrates the mercy of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). He adds that it is because of his ([emperumAnAr’s](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) infinite mercy towards him that he got some treasured qualities in him. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) starts by saying that they (himself and his SrIvaishNava associates) was chosen as the target of periya perumAL’s infinite blessings. They got the glorious opportunity of being in [SrIrangam](http://acharya.org/dd/a/srirangam.html), the chief of all [108 dhivya dhESams](https://koyil.org/). They got the rare blessings to eat, drink, breathe [nammAzhvAr’s](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) works day in and day out. They got the choicest blessings to live by the tenets propounded by [madhurakavi Azhvar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/madhurakavi-azhwar/), i.e,. charama parva nishtai (regarding one’s AchAryan as everything). This happens to the rarest of the rarest cases. They got to explore and live by the words of their ancestors who in fact lived by the words of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/). They also did not go anywhere else apart from SrIvaishNava scriptures. They spent their lives living by it. Lastly, but most importantly, if they were to meet such a SrIvaishNava with all these aforementioned qualities, they would never get an iota of jealousy in them. They would be very happy about them. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says that all these fortunes that they got is solely due to the blessings of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).

#### **Explanation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says, “We became the target of the causeless mercy of periya perumAL, who is reclining south facing in the direction of Sri Lanka, in a place that is very pleasing to the eyes and is known by the name of “kOyil”, where HE captivated HIS devotees by blessing them (“*aruL koduthittu adiyavarai AtkkoLvAn amarum Ur* ([periyAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyazhwar/) thirumozhi 4.9.3). We got the glorious opportunity of being permanent residents of [SrIrangam](http://acharya.org/dd/a/srirangam.html) that is described as “*thennAdum vadanAdum thozha ninRa thiruvarangam thiruppadhi* ([periyAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyazhwar/) thirumozhi 4.9.11)”, “*ArAmam sUzhndha arangam* ([siriya thirumadal](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/) 71)”, “*thalaiyarangam* ([iraNdAm thiruvandhAdhi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/bhuthaththazhwar/) 70)”. It is the chief of all the [108 dhivyadhESams](https://koyil.org/). Our food is the nectarine pAsurams of (nectarine for devotees that serves as garland for the Lord) [nammAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/), who is full of auspicious qualities starting with parabhakthi etc. We attained the last frontier of “charama parva nishtai”, that is celebrated as “*yathIndhramEva nIrandhram hishEvE dhaivathambaram*” etc. Myself and my associates started to talk about it “*unnaiyozhiya oru dheyvam maRRaRiyA mannupugazh sEr [vaduganambi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vaduga-namb) thannilaiyai* ([Arththi prabandham 11](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/07/arththi-prabandham-11/)”). This tenet of charama parva nishtai (regarding one’ AchAryan as everything) is derived from the) divine words of [madhurakavi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/madhurakavi-azhwar/) who said “*thEvu maRRaRiyEn* ([kaNNinun chiruth thAmbu 2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/?p=1309))”. We got to live and abide by the tenets of the great [madhurakavi AzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/madhurakavi-azhwar/), who is described as “*avargaLaich chiriththiruppAr oruvar uNdirE* ([SrIvachana bhUshaNam](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) 409) referring to madhurakavi AzhvAr (He is a person who would laugh at the 10 AzhvArs because of lack of reliability in their approach towards reaching perumAL. Their approach is via perumAL himself whereas in the case of [madhurakavi AzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/madhurakavi-azhwar/) everything is [nammAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) for him). We got to live, breathe and explore our ancestors’s works, their divine and esoteric purports. These are the works of [AchAryas](http://acharyas.koyil.org/) who lived by the way shown by [AzhvArs.](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) We spent our times dwelling on those (works). Our minds do not go to anything that is not these divine works of our ancestors. Our hearts and minds were so grounded to these works of our ancestors that it never went behind any of the other works apart from our ancestors’ works.

If the aforementioned qualities of ours that we got by the grace of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is placed on one side of a balance, then this one that I am going to say would equal or weigh more than all of the above together. If such a rare SrIvaishnava is found with all of the aforementioned qualities thus far in this pAsuram, as described by “*ippadi irukkum SrIvaishNavargaL ERRam aRindhu ugandhu irukkaiyum* ([mumukshupadi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) dwayaprakaNam 116)”, then we never get any jealous seeing them. Such is our glory that was bestowed upon us by [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). We got this! Alas! What a great fortune to have gotten this, thanks to [emperumAnAr’s](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) causeless mercy.


## Arththi prabandham – ५६
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-55/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/ramanujar-mamunigal.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/ramanujar-mamunigal.jpg)

**Introduction**

In the previous pAsuram, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) said “*madhurakavi sorppadiyE nilayAgap peRROm*”. In relation to that and as a logical next step to it, in this pAsuram, he requests for eternal service at the lotus feet of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).

**pAsuram 56**

*undhan abhimAnamE uththArakam enRu*  
*sindhai theLindhirukka cheydha nI*  
*andhO yathirAsA! nOygaLal ennai nalakkAmal*  
*sadhirAga nin thiruththAL thA*

#### **Word-by-Word Meanings**

[ethirAsA](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! – hey the leader of yathis (ascetics)!!!  
undhan abhimAnamE uththArakam enRu – As [piLLai lOkAchAryar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/pillai-lokacharyar/) says “*AchArya abhimAnamE uththArakam* (SrI vachana bhUshaNam 447), the devotion and care that you (emperumAnAr) have towards me is the sole determining factor for a soul’s upliftment.  
sindhai theLindhirukka cheydha nI – This point has been etched in my mind forever. As they say, “*theLivuRRa sindhaiyar* (thiruvAimozhi 7.5.11)”, you (emperumAnAr) had blessed my heart to be pure (without any dirt) forever.  
andhO – Alas!!!  
thA – You have to bestow  
ennai – me  
sadhirAga – intelligently  
nin thiruththAL – (with service) to your lotus feet  
nalakkAmal – without being affected  
nOygaLal – with sufferings

#### **Simple Translation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) requests kainkaryam at the lotus feet of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). This is following to what he said in the previous pAsuram “*[madhurakavi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) sorppadiyE nilayAgap peRROm*”. He says that it was [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who bestowed him with the knowledge about “what AchAryan thinks about you and how much devoted he is about you is what matters”. Even this knowledge is able to live in my mind and heart through his grace. Alas! He requests all his sufferings to end and requests [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) to smartly make a move and take him unto his lotus feet.

#### **Explanation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says “hey! the leader of yathis. You are the person who preached and bestowed me with the knowledge of the phrase “*AchArya abhimAnamE uththArakam* ([srivachanabhUshaNam](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) 447). Based on that, your love and devotion towards me counts as everything for me. This philosophy has been so rooted in me as described in “*theLivuRRa sindhaiyar* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 7.5.11)”. With your blessings, I am living by it. Alas! Please do not make me suffer more with pains in this world. As you said in [SaraNAgathi gadhyam](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/saranagathi-gadhyam/), “*sukhEnEmAm prakruthim sthUla sUkshma rUpAm visrujya*”, you should take me intelligently to your lotus feet and bless me with eternal service to them as per “*un padha yugamAm yEr koNda vIdu* ([rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi 83](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-83/)).


## Arththi prabandham – ५७
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-56/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/emperumAnAr-thiruvAimozhippiLLai-mAmunigaL.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/emperumAnAr-thiruvAimozhippiLLai-mAmunigaL.jpg)

**Introduction**

[mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) in this pAsuram, assumes that [SrI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/emperumanar/) has a question in his mind and answers him in this pAsuram. The imaginary question that mAmunigaL thinks is running in SrI rAmAnuja’s head is as follows. SrI rAmAnuja asks, “hey mAmunigaL! I have heard your requests. You ask me to do a list of things. Can I ask you something? On what basis/recommendation do you ask me? Do you have any strong background / recommendation for your claims? Is there anyone?”. To this question mAmunigaL answers, “Yes. I deemed myself as a thing in the first place after having surrendered to my AchAryan ‘[thiruvAimozhip piLLai’](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/). That is my greatest qualification. Please consider that sole diamond I have. Hey emperumAnAre! You do not look at my flaws. As they say, ‘*yathIsvara SruNu Sriman krupayA parayA thava’*, please lend your ears toward my low words”.

**pAsuram 57**

*dhEsigargaL pORRum thiruvAimozhip piLLai*  
*vAsamalar thAL adaindha vaththuvennum*  
*nEsaththAl en pizhaigaL kANA ethirAsarE*  
*adiyEn punpagarvai kELum poRuththu*

**Word-by-Word Meanings:**

vAsamalar thAL adaindha vaththuvennum – I am a thing (vasthu) who surrendered at the divinely fragrant and soft lotus feet of  
dhEsigargaL pORRum thiruvAimozhip piLLai – [thiruvAimozhip piLLai,](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) who is celebrated by ancestors as “*senthamizh vEdhath thirumalaiyAzhvAr vAzhi*”. HE is the person who expressed deep and unshakable servitude to [nammAzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) and his scriptures. He spent his livelihood dwelling on nammAzhvAr’s nectarine pAsurams.  
nEsaththAl – Because of this association  
ethirAsarE – emperumAnArE!!!  
kELum – please listen to  
adiyEn – my  
punpagarvai – lowly words  
en pizhaigaL kANA – without seeing my flaws and not focusing about it at all  
poRuththu – and without bursting out

**Simple Translation**

mAmunigaL requests SrI rAmAnuja to look at the great association the former has with [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) (his AchAryan). He asks SrI rAmAnuja to ignore his flaws, and listen to his lowly words without expressing any burst of anger.

**Explanation**

mAmunigal says to SrI rAmAnuja, “I am a thing (vasthu) who surrendered at the divinely fragrant and soft lotus feet of [thiruvAimozhip piLLai,](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) who is celebrated by ancestors as “*senthamizh vEdhath thirumalayAzhvAr vAzhi*”. HE is the person who expressed deep and unshakeable servitude to nammAzhvAr and his scriptures. He spent his livelihood dwelling on nammAzhvAr’s nectarine pAsurams.

emperumAnArE!!! Because of this association, please listen to my lowly words without seeing my flaws and not focusing about it at all and without bursting out.


## Arththi prabandham – ५८
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:
