[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-57/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/emperumanar-1.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/06/emperumanar-1.jpg)

#### **Introduction**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) in his last pAsuram said “*thiruvAimozhip piLLai vAsamalarth thAL adaindha vaththu*”. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) celebrated himself as a “vasthu” (an entity in the first place) that sought the lotus feet of t[hiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/). He says that there is more to it. It is because of his association with [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) (AchAryan – Sishya relationship), he was able to recognize, appreciate and understand the significance of the relationship with [SrI rAmAnujA](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).

#### **pAsuram 58**

*endhai thiruvAimozhip piLLai innaruLAl*  
*undhan uRavai uNarththiya pin indha uyirkku*  
*ellA uRavum nI enRE ethirAsA*  
*nillAdhadhu uNdO en nenju*

#### **Word-by-Word Meanings**

endhai – ([mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says) “There is a popular phrase that goes like “*thirumanthram mAthAvum, pithA AchAryanum enRu aruLich cheyvargaL*”. Based on that my father [thiruVaimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/).  
[thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) – his  
innaruLAl – causeless mercy  
undhan uRavai – (made me understand) all kinds of relations at your ([SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s) lotus feet  
indha uyirkku – that this soul shares.  
uNarththiya pin – After protecting me by making me realize my ignorance in the first place,  
ethirAsA – [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)!!!  
nI enRE – Isn’t it you?  
ellA uRavum – who is referred in all the possible relationships that are implicit in [thirumanthram](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2015/12/rahasya-thrayam.html)?  
en nenju nillAdhadhu uNdO – (Having said that) Will there ever be a condition when, my heart will be wavering? (The answer is an obvious no). It behooves us to take cognizance of the opportune phrases in “*thandhai naRRAi thAram thanayar perunjelvam endhanakku nIyE*” and “*allAdha suRRamumAgi*”

#### **Simple Translation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says that it is because of his AchAryan and spiritual father [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)’s grace that he was able to realize all the different relationship that his soul shares with [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). His grace removed all the ignorance he had hitherto and thereby protecting him. After this, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) questions will there ever be a condition when his heart would be wavering? The answer is a clear no.

#### **Explanation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says, “There is a popular phrase that goes like “*thirumanthram mAthAvum, pithA AchAryanum enRu aruLich cheyvargaL*”. Based on that my spiritual father [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)’s causeless mercy made me understand, all kinds of relations at your ([SrI rAmAnuja’](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)s) lotus feet that this soul shares. Hey [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)!!! After protecting me by making me realize my ignorance in the first place, isn’t it you who is referred in all the possible relationships that are implicit in thirumanthram? Having said that, will there ever be a condition when, my heart will be wavering? (The answer is an obvious no). It behooves us to take cognizance of the opportune phrases in “*thandhai naRRAi thAran thanayar perunjelvam endhanakku nIyE* ([Arththi prabandham 3](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/06/arththi-prabandham-3/))” and “*allAdha suRRamumAgi* ([Arththi prabandham 54](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-54/))”.


## Arththi prabandham – ५९
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-58/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/going-to-paramapadham.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/going-to-paramapadham.jpg)

#### **Introduction**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says “I understood the relationship between me and your lotus feet (thanks to my AchAryan [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)). When will you destroy this mortal coil of mine, after which [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) (who does things that is the best for the soul) comes on garudan and displays HIS face to me? [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), please tell me when you will do that?”

#### **pAsuram 59**

*endhai thiruvarangar ErAr garudan mEl*  
*vandhu mugam kAtti vazhi nadaththach chindhai seydhu*  
*ippollA udambuthanai pOkkuvadhu ennALkolo?*  
*sollAy ethirAsA! sUzhndhu!!!*

**Word-by-Word Meanings:**

endhai – (During the time when this soul leaves the body) my mother and father  
thiruvarangar – i.e., [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/), who is known through his dwelling place of kOyil ([SrIrangam](http://acharya.org/dd/a/srirangam.html))  
mugam kAtti –, will show my favorite aspects that include HIS kasthUri thilakam, smiling face etc.  
vandhu – by coming unto me  
ErAr garudan mEl – on top of HIS beautiful garudan.  
vazhi nadaththa – and usher me into the glorious path known as “archirAdhi mArgam”  
ethirAsA! – [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)  
sollAy – please tell me  
ippollA udambuthanai pOkkuvadhu ennALkolo? – When is the day that this despicable body of mine will get destroyed and the soul will bedeemed for you?  
chindhai seydhu – Please think about  
sUzhndhu – and elucidate me on that so that I will be happy about the concreteness of it. Please think about it.

#### **Simple Translation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) asks for the exact day when [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) will take his body and liberate his soul, to be dedicated exclusively to him. He asks when has he decided for that to happen. He also describes what will happen during his final moments. He says that [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/), who is at [SrIrangam](http://acharya.org/dd/a/srirangam.html), will come on top of HIS beautiful garudan and usher him to HIS paramapadham via “*archirAdhi mArgam*”.

#### **Explanation**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) asks, “hey! [SrI rAmAnuja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! When is the day that you are going to destroy this body of mine that is the sole determinant to be liberated? During the time the soul leaves the body, I will see my mother and father [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) whose sheer existence is revealed by his dwelling in “kOyil” or “[SrIrangam](http://acharya.org/dd/a/srirangam.html)”. HE will come on top of HIS extremely beautiful garudan that is described as “*am chirai puL pAgan* ([thirunedunthANdagam](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) 6)”. HE will show me my favorite aspects that include the likes of HIS kasthUri thilakam, HIS beautiful smile that is described as *“nal kadhir muththa veNNagaich cheyavAy* ([periya thirumozhi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) 4.4.5) and HIS moon like face. HE, who is described as “the lovable companion at [SrIrangam](http://acharya.org/dd/a/srirangam.html)” or “*arangathuRaiyum inthuNaivanAna thAm* ([periya thirumozhi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) 3.7.6)”, will usher me to paramapadham as in “*nayAmi paramAm gatham* ([varAha charama SlOlam](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2015/12/rahasya-thrayam.html)) via the path known as “*archirAdhi mArgam*”. As [nammAzhvAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/18/nammazhwar/) said “*un charaNam thandhu en sanmam kaLaiyAyE* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 5.8.7)”, [emperumAnArE](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)!!! When are you going to offer your lotus feet to me and put a full stop to my cycle of birth and deaths forever? When are you going to take my body and make this soul exclusively for you? In SrI rAmAyaNam, SrI rAma was given a clear cut time of 14 years to come back to HIS kingdom of ayOdhya in the phrase *“pUrNE chathurdhasE varshE”*. bharatha was consoled by this as he had a definitive time frame as to when SrI rAma would be back. As per the phrase *“ArurOharatham hrushta:*” he was able to get some happiness because of the light at the end of a tunnel. However, I am not able to bear any more of these consolatory times. So, please tell an answer that will make me happy. The word “sUzhndhu” here has the same connotation when it was used in the phrase “*avAvarach chUzh*” ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.10.11) and “*sollu nIyAm aRiyach chUzndhu* ([periya thiruvandhAdhi](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/18/nammazhwar/) 16)”.


## Arththi prabandham – ६०
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/arththi-prabandham/)

[\<\< Previous](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2017/03/arththi-prabandham-59/)

[![](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/12/ramanuja.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/12/ramanuja.jpg)

#### **Introduction**

[mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) thinks to himself, “Why do we have to yearn for our goal/objective anymore? Everything that [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) had bestowed [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) with, will automatically be applicable to us as well, as we are at the lotus feet of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). It automatically applies to us because we are the children of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)”. Thus, in this final pAsuram, [mAmunigAL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) is extremely gleeful as he is bestowed with all the things that [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) was given by [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/).

**maNavALa mAmunigAL thiruvadigaLE SaraNam!!!**

#### **pAsuram 60**

*indha arangaththu inidhu iru nIyenRu arangar*  
*endhai ethirAsarkkIndha varam sindhai seyyil*  
*nammadhanRO nenjame naRRAdhai sompudhalvar*  
*thammadhanRO thAyamuRai thAn*

#### **Word-by-Word meanings**

arangar – [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/)  
indha arangaththu – in this kOyil ([SrIrangam](http://acharya.org/dd/a/srirangam.html))  
inidhu iru nIyenRu – told “SrIrangE sukhamAsva” (be happily settled in SrIrangam)  
endhai ethirAsarkku – to my father emperumAnAr.  
nenjamE – Hey my heart!!!  
sindhai seyyil – If we were to thinking about this  
indha varam – precious boon that was bestowed by periya perumAL to emperumAnAr  
nammadhanRO – isn’t it true that the boon is actually ours too?  
naRRAdhai – emperumAnAr is our causeless father.  
thAyamuRai thAn – Because one’s parents’  
sompudhalvar thammadhanRO – properties are automatically transferred to the sons.

([mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) says to his heart, “Hey! my dear heart. Hence, we do not have to do anything on our part. Everything is readily available by default. Our burden is not a burden anymore for us (implying that [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) will take care of the burden and that he in fact has taken care of [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) by granting him his wish).

#### **Concluding Note**

[periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) bestowed [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) with both HIS wealth namely nithya vibhUthi (paramapadham) and leelA vibhUthi (all the remaining places that are not paramapadham). Hence, [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is celebrated as “SrI vishNu lOka maNi maNdapa mArgadhAyi” (dhAti panchakam 5). emperumAnAr is the leader of all prapannas. It is such [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), that jIyar who is also known as “[maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)”, “yathIndra pravaNar”, surrendered himself totally. He performed prapaththi to [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). He got the ultimate goal of going to paramapadham and doing eternal kainkaryam to bhagavAn (and bhAgavathAs). This would mean, this same result would be bestowed to everyone who has the abhimAnam of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). This effectively means that everyone who has surrendered unto the lotus feet of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) would beget his love in the first place upon which they will be transcended to infinite bliss in paramapadham once and for all.

#### **Simple Translation**

In this final pAsuram, [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) is very happy because he knows that everything that he had asked for is readily available to him, thanks to his association with [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). This was possible in the first place because [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) had literally granted everything to [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) earlier as revealed by the verses in [gadhya thrayam](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/saranagathi-gadhyam/). As a child of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) is very happy that all the boons (kainkaryam starting from the remainder of this life to doing kainkaryam at paramapdham) that [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) bestowed [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) will be enjoyed by him (mAmunigaL) as well.

#### **Explanation**

[mAmunigal](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) tells his heart, “hey! My dear heart! Remember what [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) told our father [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! Remember HIS words from [SaraNAgathi gadhyam](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/saranagathi-gadhyam/). Firstly HE told, “dhvayam arthAnusandhAnEna sahasadhaivam vakthA yAvachcharIra pAdham aththraiva [SrIrangE sukhamAsva](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/02/saranagathi-gadhyam-19/)”. After this, HE said something that starts from “*SarIra pAdha samayEthu*” and ending with “[nithyakinkarO bhavishyasi mAthE bhUthathra samsaya: ithi mayayvahyuktham athasthvam thava thathvathO mathgyAna dharShanaprApthishU nissamsaya: sukhamAsva](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/02/saranagathi-gadhdyam-21-23/)”. [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) clearly bestowed our father [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) with everything needed to continue the reminder of his journey of life in this world as well as what he would get once he leaves this earth (which is nothing but kainkaryam in paramapadham). [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) HIMSELF gave all these boon to [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). If we were to closely examine this boon, we, the children of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), will automatically be entitled to these boons. This is because, all the properties of parents is automatically inherited by their children. Hence, my dear heart! We do not have to strive for anything on our own any longer. Everything is available readily to us, thanks to [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi-english/) bestowed [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) with both HIS wealth namely nithya vibhUthi (paramapadham) and leelA vibhUthi (all the remaining places that are not paramapadham). Hence, [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is celebrated as “*SrI vishNu lOka maNi maNdapa mArgadhAyi*” (dhAti panchakam 5). [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is the leader of all prapannas. Towards such [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), [jIyar](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) who is also known as “[maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/)”, “yathIndra pravaNar”, surrendered himself totally. He performed prapaththi to [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). He got the ultimate thing of going to paramapadham and doing eternal kainkaryam to bhagavAn (and bhAgavathas). This would mean, this same result would be bestowed to everyone who has the abhimAnam of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). This effectively means that everyone who has surrendered unto the lotus feet of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) would beget his love as a starting point, upon which they will be transcended to infinite bliss in paramapadham once and for all.

There are lots of times when [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) exclaims “[ethirAsA](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! [ethirAsA](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)!”. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) sends the message that [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is the leader of yathis. All his Sishyas heap praises on their leader “[yathirAja](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)” by chanting his names constantly. [mAmunigaL](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) feels that he is also one among the Sishyas and hence he is also entitled to chant his names constantly as per “yadhyassudhasathvA:”. Hence, [mAmunigal](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) always advocates to tell his name “[ethirAsa](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)! [ethirAsA](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)”.

**jIyar thiruvadigaLE SaraNam**


## 


## 


## thiruvAimozhi – २.८.४ – pulan aindhum
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/?page_id=23 "thiruvAimozhi – Fourth 1000") \>\> [Second Centum](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/thiruvaimozhi-2nd-centum/ "thiruvAimozhi – 1st centum") \>\> [Eighth decad](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/thiruvaimozhi-2-8-anaivadhu/)

[Previous pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/thiruvaimozhi-2-8-3-punarkkum-ayanam/)

[![paramapadhanathan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/paramapadhanathan.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/paramapadhanathan.jpg)

#### **Introduction for this pAsuram**

**Highlights from [thirukkurukaippirAn piLLAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/pillan/)‘s introduction**

No specific introduction.

**Highlights from [nanjIyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nanjiyar/)‘s introduction**

In the fourth pAsuram – [AzhwAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) says “Oh ones who desire eternal goal of liberation in the form of unsurpassed happiness after giving up attachment to petty worldly pleasures! You take refuge of [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)“.

**Highlights from [vAdhi kEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar/)‘s introduction**

Subsequently, [AzhwAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) says “To attain [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) after being relieved from this samsAram (material realm), you immerse in the auspicious qualities of such [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) always”.

**Highlights from [periyavAchchAn piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyavachchan-pillai/)‘s introduction**

In the fourth pAsuram – [AzhwAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) says “Oh ones who desire for liberation after cutting off the ties in this material realm on meditating upon [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) of such nature! You immerse in his auspicious qualities”.

**Highlights from [nampiLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nampillai/)‘s introduction as documented by [vadakkuth thiruvIdhip piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vadakku-thiruvidhi-pillai/)  **

Fourth pAsuram. There was no defect in [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/)‘s supremacy \[as seen in previous pAsuram\]. Now, AzhwAr says “Oh ones who wish to attain a benefit which has no equal! See that you quickly accept him as refuge”.

#### **pAsuram**

*pulan aindhu mEyum poRi aindhu nIngi*  
*nalam andham illadhOr nAdu puguvIr!*  
*alamandhu vIya asuraraich cheRRAn*  
*palamundhu sIril padiminOvAdhE  *

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/thiruvaimozhi-2-8-4)

#### **Word-by-Word meanings (based on [vAdhi kEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar/)‘s 12000 padi)**

pulan – visible matters  
aindhum – in those five  
mEyum – well-fitting  
poRi – like a trap which catches him  
aindhum – from the five senses  
nIngi – detaching  
nalam – bliss  
andhamilladhu – being unlimited  
Or – distinct/unique  
nAdu – in the abode  
puguvIr – Oh the ones who desire to enter!  
alamandhu – toiling  
vIya – be destroyed  
asurarai – demons  
seRRAn – of the one who killed  
mundhu – from the beginning  
palam – being the result (due to its sweetness)  
sIril – in the auspicious qualities  
OvAdhE – always  
padimin – be immersed

#### **Simple translation (based on [vAdhi kEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar/)‘s 12000 padi)**

Oh the ones who desire to be detached from the five sense organs (ears, skin, eyes, nose and tongue) which trap him ([AthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)) completely in the five matters (sound, touch, vision, smell and taste) and to enter the abode of unlimited bliss! [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) who killed the demons that were destroyed after toiling hard – you always be immersed in the auspicious qualities of such emperumAn which can be explained as the result (due to its sweetness) from the beginning.

#### vyAkyAnams (commentaries)

**Highlights from [thirukkurukaippirAn piLLAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/pillan/)‘s vyAkyAnam**

See [vAdhi kEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar/)‘s translation.

**Highlights from [nanjIyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nanjiyar/)‘s vyAkyAnam  **

See [nampiLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nampillai/)‘s vyAkyAnam.

**Highlights from [periyavAchchAn piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyavachchan-pillai/)‘s vyAkyAnam**

See [nampiLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nampillai/)‘s vyAkyAnam.

**Highlights from [nampiLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nampillai/)‘s vyAkyAnam as documented by [vadakkuth thiruvIdhip piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vadakku-thiruvidhi-pillai/)  **

- *pulan …* – pulan aindhu means the five different matters (sound,
  touch, vision, smell and taste) and poRi aindhu are the sense organs
  (ears, skin, eyes, nose and tongue) which get trapped in those
  matters; being detached from them. Rats etc are killed by keeping a
  trap of certain fragrant substances; similarly the sense organs get
  trapped in the matters and become finished – so the sense organs are
  called trap. This implies that one is getting detached from being
  attached to the sense organs which can only perceive visible
  (physical) matters.
- *nalam …* – Oh ones who desire to enter the abode where there is no
  end of bliss/goodness!
  [AzhwAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) being the
  most authoritative person mercifully explains that there is a divine
  abode which has endless bliss that is to be attained to discard the
  philosophy which advocates “becoming void as liberation”.
- *puguvIr* – [AzhwAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/)
  says that our acceptance is the only qualification \[for liberation\].

Even if there is a divine abode and if an [AthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/) has the desire to enter that divine abode, if there are strong obstacles, how would one reach the divine abode?

- *alamandhu vIya asuraraich cheRRAn* –
  [AzhwAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) asks “Is it
  our job to remove the obstacles?”.
  [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)
  destroyed the demons so that they suffer and fall down \[Similarly, he
  will remove our obstacles\].
- *palamundhu sIril padimin* – You engage in his auspicious activities
  which are enjoyable right from the beginning, viz., right when we
  start pursuing them. This is explained in bhagavath gIthA 9.2 “…
  *susukam karthumavyayam*” (imperishable and very joyful to perform) –
  due to the object of meditation
  ([bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/)),
  from the beginning, it is enjoyable to perform.
- *OvAdhE* – There is no rule that one can come in contact with
  sea/ocean only during special days (month beginning, paurNami
  (full-moon day) etc) – try to engage in bhagavAn’s qualities always
  without any distraction. It can also be said as
  [AzhwAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) encouraging
  others to engage in bhagavAn’s qualities continuously since he enjoyed
  them very much. Just as it is said in periya thirumozhi 6.10.6 “*nAnum
  sonnEn namarum uraimin*” (as I have recited, let my friends/relatives
  also recite).

In the next article we will enjoy the next pAsuram.


## thiruvAimozhi – २.८.५ – OvAth thuyar
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/?page_id=23 "thiruvAimozhi – Fourth 1000") \>\> [Second Centum](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/thiruvaimozhi-2nd-centum/ "thiruvAimozhi – 1st centum") \>\> [Eighth decad](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/thiruvaimozhi-2-8-anaivadhu/)

[Previous pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/thiruvaimozhi-2-8-4-pulan-aindhum/)

[![hayagriva](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/05/hayagriva.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/05/hayagriva.jpg)

#### **Introduction for this pAsuram**

**Highlights from [thirukkurukaippirAn piLLAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/pillan/)‘s introduction**

No specific introduction.

**Highlights from [nanjIyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nanjiyar/)‘s introduction**

In the fifth pAsuram – [AzhwAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) elaborates [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)‘s *sarvasajAthIyathvam* (being born in all species) saying “emperumAn would mercifully incarnate as hayagrIva et al to protect the universes created by him”.

**Highlights from [vAdhi kEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar/)‘s introduction**

Subsequently, [AzhwAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) mercifully explains the unique nature of the many incarnations assumed by [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) who is the cause of all to protect the result of his creation.

**Highlights from [periyavAchchAn piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyavachchan-pillai/)‘s introduction**

See [nanjIyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nanjiyar/)‘s introduction.

**Highlights from [nampiLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nampillai/)‘s introduction as documented by [vadakkuth thiruvIdhip piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vadakku-thiruvidhi-pillai/)  **

Fifth pAsuram. [AzhwAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) explains previously highlighted thiruvAimozhi 2.8.1 “[*iNaivanAm epportkum*](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/thiruvaimozhi-2-8-1-anaivadhu-aravanaimel/)” (would be born among all species).

#### **pAsuram**

*OvAth thuyar piRavi utpada maRRu evvevaiyum*  
*mUvAth thani mudhalAy mUvalgum kAvalOn*  
*mAvAgi AmaiyAy mInAgi mAnidamAm*  
*dhEvAdhi dhEva perumAn en thIrththanE  *

#### [Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/thiruvaimozhi-2-8-5)

#### **Word-by-Word meanings (based on [vAdhi kEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar/)‘s 12000 padi)**

OvA – continuous (without break)  
thuyar – one that gives distress  
piRavi – creation which binds AthmA to birth  
utpada – including  
maRRu – others such as sustenance, annihilation etc  
evvevaiyum – all other activities  
mUvA – effortlessly  
thani mudhalAy – being the singular cause who does not expect anyone’s help  
mUvulagum – of the (created) universe  
kAvalOn – being the protector  
dhEva – for the dhEvas (celestial beings) starting with brahmA et al  
Adhi dhEvar – for those nithyasUris who are beyond the reach (of such dhEvathAs)  
perumAn – being the lord  
en – for me  
thIrththan – like a river bank, that is easily approachable

(for the protection of such universe)  
mAvAgi – incarnating as hayagrIva (horse-headed form, who is the propagator of vEdham)  
AmaiyAy mInAgi – incarnating as kUrma (tortoise) and mathsya (fish) (who are propagators of purANas)  
mAnidamAm – and also incarnated as human form (who is the propagator of gIthOpanishath – bhagavath gIthA)

#### **Simple translation (based on [vAdhi kEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar/)‘s 12000 padi)**

[emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) is the effortless singular cause of the created universe, without expecting anyone’s help. He is the protector of such universe which gives continuous distress for the AthmA, continuously by binding it to the universe. He is also in control of all other activities including
sustenance, annihilation etc. He is the lord for those nithyasUris who are beyond the reach of the dhEvas (celestial beings) starting with brahmA et al and is like a river bank that is easily approachable by me. Such emperumAn (for the protection of such universe) incarnates as hayagrIva (horse-headed form, who is the propagator of vEdham), as kUrma (tortoise) and mathsya (fish) (who are propagators of purANas) and also incarnated as human form (who is the propagator of gIthOpanishath – bhagavath gIthA).  
This pAsuram elaborates thiruvAimozhi 2.8.1 “[*iNaivanAm epportkum*](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/thiruvaimozhi-2-8-1-anaivadhu-aravanaimel/)” (would be born among all species).

#### vyAkyAnams (commentaries)

**Highlights from [thirukkurukaippirAn piLLAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/pillan/)‘s vyAkyAnam**

See [vAdhi kEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar/)‘s translation.

**Highlights from [nanjIyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nanjiyar/)‘s vyAkyAnam  **

See [nampiLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nampillai/)‘s vyAkyAnam.

**Highlights from [periyavAchchAn piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyavachchan-pillai/)‘s vyAkyAnam**

See [nampiLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nampillai/)‘s vyAkyAnam.

**Highlights from [nampiLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nampillai/)‘s vyAkyAnam as documented by [vadakkuth thiruvIdhip piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vadakku-thiruvidhi-pillai/)  **

- *OvAth thuyar piRavi utpada …* – Before he said in [thiruvAimozhi
  2.8.2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/05/thiruvaimozhi-2-8-2-nindhum-thuyar/)
  “*nIndhum thuyarp piRavi*” (sorrowful birth etc which are difficult to
  cross-over); here he says – it is not just something that gives us
  opportunities to recoup and escape – it is those six aspects (jAyathE
  – birth, asthi – existence, pariNamathE – change, vivardhathE –
  growth, apakshIyathE – decay, naSyathi – disappearance) and the
  objects of such aspects which cause continuous sorrows.
- *mUvAth thanimudhal – mUvA* – without laziness, effortlessly; this is
  explained as adjective for both “*OvAth thuyar piRavi utpada*” and
  *“thani mudhal*“, that is,
  [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/)
  being the singular cause without laziness for these six aspects which
  go on eternally in continuity (*pravAha rUpaththAlE nithyam*) and
  being the effortless singular cause of these entire creations. Though
  [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)
  gives body/senses to AthmAs to facilitate them to worship him, if they
  misuse the tools, he would think “if they do like this, let me develop
  their taste towards me over time”, will allow them to continue in
  their path and be neutral/indifferent towards them. Thus, even if they
  digress from his own desire (of accepting all of them), like a farmer
  who would try growing crops again and again instead of giving up, he
  keeps engaging in creation again and again. This is explained in
  periya thiruvanthAdhi 18 “*sOmbAdhu ippal uruvai ellAm padarviththa
  viththA*” (without laziness, you, who are the original cause who
  created this universe that has variegated aspects).

What is he creating and protecting?

- *mUvulagum kAvalOn* – whatever that is in the boundary of the material
  realm. Two explanations for mUvulagam:
  - 3 layers – Lower layer (seven worlds below bhUmi (earth) – athala,
    vithala, …, pAthAla), middle layer (Earth), upper layer (six worlds
    above earth – bhuva:, svarga, maha:, jana:, thapa:, sathya).
  - 3 types of worlds – kruthakam (3 worlds below mahar lOkam – bhU:
    (earth), bhUva:, svarga) – these are recreated as part of each
    manvanthra (life of manu – 71 chathur yugams approximately),
    akruthakam (3 worlds above mahar lOkam) – jana:, thapa:, sathya –
    these remain undisturbed even during the dissolution of a
    manvanthra, kruthakAkruthakam (maharlOkam) – this gets recreated at
    a lesser frequency \[during the beginning of brahmA’s day which
    contains 1000 chathur yugams\] \[Here the context of recreation is
    within the boundary of brahmA’s one day\].
- *kAvalOn* – Protecting by propagating SAsthram etc.

Does he protect without minimizing his supremacy?

- *mAvAgi …* – akarmavaSya (one who is not bound by karma) being born
  amongst / like karmavaSya (one who is bound by karma).
- *mAvAgi* – incarnated as hayagrIva mUrththi (horse headed form).
- *AmaiyAy mInAgi* – incarnations which are focussed on revealing
  sacred/true knowledge.
- *mAnidamAm* – incarnations such as SrI rAma, krishNa et al. As
  explained in SrI rAmAyaNam sundhara kANdam 35.11 “*maryAdhAnAm cha
  lOkasya karthA kArayithA cha sa:*” (That SrI rAma is the epitome of
  maintaining honour/dignity and one who engages others to be
  honourable/dignified) and in bhagavath gIthA 3.21 “*yadhyadhAcharathi
  SrEshta: …*” (whatever performed by great person, common men will
  follow…”.

Who is the person who makes himself available in such mortal forms?

- *dhEvAdhi dhEva perumAn* – He is beyond the reach of nithyasUris who
  cannot handle the smell/acquaintance of dhEvas (celestial beings) who
  cannot handle the smell/acquaintance of humans.
- *en thIrththanE* – two explanations:
  - pure –
    [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)
    who has the purity to purify me; he changed my desire from worldly
    matters, towards him (I was like those who desire for cheap foods
    when most delicious foods are available).
  - easily approachable – he is like the banks of a river where we can
    step in and immerse.

In the next article we will enjoy the next pAsuram.
